







































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Ntsiku ibodzi Mbuya adawuza Jona mwana wa Amitai aciti:
“Lamuka uyende ku m'zinda ukulu wa Niniva ukaupalizire thangwe ine-pano ndabzibva kale bza kuipa bzawo.”
Ndipo Jona adalamuka aciyenda kuTalisisi kuthawa Mbuya. Iye adapolika ku Jopa, kumweko adakaona xitima ya m’madzi yomwe ikhafuna kuyenda ku Talisisi. Adagula thikiti acipakira kuti ayende ku Talisisiko, Mbuya aciona na maso yawo.
Ndipo Mulungu adatumiza conzi cikulu kwene-kwene, madzi ya nyanza yadabvunduka yacicita mawimbi makulu. Ndipo xitimayo ikhadasala pang'ono kulobzika.
Wakubvukuta xitimayo adabva mantha, aciyamba kukuwa m’bodzi na m’bodzi acimbakumbira thandizo kuna mulungu wace. Ndipo iwo adayamba kuthusa mitolo m’madzi kuti xitimayo ilule. Tsono Jona adabuluka pantsi pa xitimayo acikagona tulo.
Ndipo m'kulu wa xitima adyenda kukam'bvunza Jona kuti: “Ungoneranyi muno? Lamuka, ukumbire mulungu wako! Pinango iye angatibvere ntsisi kuti tisaye kufa.
Iwo adapangana wentse kuti: “Mbatibwereni tione mbani wabweresa tsokali. Iwo adacita tenepoyo acifufudza ndipo adaphata Jona.
Pamwepo adam'bvunza kuti: “Tiwuze tsapanopa kuti thangwe lanyi taona tsokali. Uli kucitanyi muno? Ndiwe wa kuponi? Ndiwe wa m'tundu wanyi?
Ndipo Jona adatawira aciti: “Ndine mu Ebereu, nimbapemba Mulungu Mbuya wa kudzulu, omwe adalenga madzi ya nyanza na pantsi.”
Ndipo wanthuwo adabva mantha kwene-kwene acim'bvunza pomwe kuti: “Wacitiranyi bzimwebzi? Thangwe iwo akhadziwa kale kuti iye akhathawa Mbuya, omwe akhadamutuma.
Pamwepo, iwo adamubvunza aciti: “Tsono unfuna kuti tikucitenyi ife-pano kuti madzi ya nyanzaya yaderekhe?” Thangwe madzi ya nyanzayo yakhambabvunduka yacimbadzala pomwe.
Ndipo Jona adawatawira aciti: “Nditembeni mundithuse m’madzi ya nyanzaya, ndipo iyo ya n’derekha. Nakuti ine nin'dziwa kuti conzici cabwera na thangwe langu”.
Na tenepo wabvukuti akhabvukuta kan'kulumize kuti afike kamangu ku mphepete, tsono alibe kukwanisa thangwe mawimbiyo yakhana mphanvu kwene-kwene,
ndipo pamwepo adayamba kupemba na kukuwa aciti: “Nandi Mbuya! Tiri kukumbirambo kuti muleke kutipha na thangwe la munthuyu. Lekani kutipasa mulandu na thangwe la infa yace, nakuti imwepo Mbuya mwacita bzomwe imwe mwatonga.”
Iwo adam'temba Jona, acimuthusa m'madzi, kucokera pamwepo ndipo mandziyo yadaderekha.
Iwo adabva mantha kwene-kwene na Mbuya, ndipo acimuikhira ntsembe, acikhala pomwe na cikhulupiro.
Ndipo Mbuya adatumiza cintsomba cikulu kwene-kwene, kuti cimumeze Jonayo, iye adakhala ntsiku zitatu m’mimba mwacenemo.
Ndipo Jona adapemba m’mimba mwa cintsombamo kuna Mulungu wace,
aciti: “Pa kubonera kwangu, ine ndidapemba kuna Mbuya, ndipo iye adanditawira, m'kati mwa cidindi ndidakuwa ndipo mudandibva fala langu.
Imwepo mudandithusa panyanza, mphanvu ya madzi icindimiza, mawimbi mang'ono na makulu yacipita na padzulu pangu”.
Ine ndidalewa kuti: “Ndathusidwa imwe muciona, na tenepo nin'dzaiona pomwe nyumba yanu ya kucena.”
Madzi yadandimiza ya cifuna kundipha, m’dima udandigwanankhira, na mabonga yacindiyanga mum'solo.
Ine-pano ndidabuluka pantsi pakuzika pa kuyambira mapiri, mphinga za m’suwo wa infa zidandifungira pa nthawe zentse. Tsono imwepo Mbuya Mulungu mundandipulumusa moyo wangu pa infa.
Pomwe ndikhatsindira moyo, ine ndidakukumbukani imwepo Mbuya. Ndidakupemberani, ndipo mafala yanguyo yadafika m’nyumba mwanu mwa kucena.
Wale omwe ambapemba bzifanikiso bza kusaya basa, ambaphonya cilungamo canu.
Tsono ine nin'dzakupasani ntsembe na kukomedwa kwangu; ndicidzandendemeza cikhulupiriso cangu. Nakuti cipulumuso cimbacokera kuna Mbuya.
Ndipo Mbuya adaciwuza cinstombaco, kuti cimubzukule kunja Jona.
Ndipo Mbuya adamuwuza pomwe Jona kaciwiri kuti:
“Lamuka uyende ku m'zinda ukulu wa Niniva ukaupalizire mafala yomwe ndakuwuzaya.”
Ndipo iye adayenda ku Ninivako, ninga momwe adamuwuzira Mbuya. Tsono Niniva ukhali m'zinda ukulu omwe ukhana m'thantho wa ntsiku zitatu kuti auyambuke na minyendo.
Pomwe Jona adapita mum'zindamo, adafamba ntsiku yentse acimbapaliza acimbalewa kuti: “M'kati mwa ntsiku makumi manai, Niniva in'pfudzidwa.”
Wanthu wentse wa m'Ninivamo, akulu na wana adabvuma Mulungu. Iwo adapangana kuti abzimane kudya, acibvala mausakala kuyambira nkulu mpaka mwana.
Pomwe mambo wa ku Niniva adaibva nkhani imweyo, adalekeza basa lace la umambo, acikabvalambo mausakala, na kukabvunvulikambo pa dotha.
Iye adadziwisa wanthu wentse wa mu m'zindamo mu dzina lace, na la nthena zace Kuti: “Palibe munthu m’bodzi yekha omwe anidya, ayai kumwa cinthu; kudyesa na kumwesa bzifuwo, zingakhale ng'ombe ayai mbuzi.
Tsono wanthu na bzifuwo kubodzi an'dzabvala mausakala acipemba na mphanvu kuna Mulungu, acileka kucita bza kuipa bzawo, na kuleka pomwe kuphana wokha-wokha.
Kodi mbani an'dziwa kuti Mulungu angatibvera ntsisi, acipepa ukali bwace; kuti tisaye kufa?
Thangwe Mulungu adaona, kuti iwo aleka kucita bza kuipa bzawo, aciwabvera ntsisi, acileka kucita bzomwe akhadakumbuka kuti awacitebzo. Ndipo iye alibe kubzicita.
Tsono Jona alibe kukomedwa nabzo bzimwebzo, ndipo iye adakalipa.
Iye adapemba kuna Mbuya aciti: “Nandi Mbuya! Kodi n'psimwebzi lini bzomwe ndikhadalewa kale, pomwe ndikhali kumui?” Ndipopo ine ndikhadathabza, ndicithawa ndicikuyenda ku Talisisi. Nakuti ine-pano ndikhadziwa kale kuti iwepo ndiwe Mulungu wa kudeka m'tima, wa nsisi kwene-kwene, wa kufewa m'tima na wa kupirira pomwe, omwe umbalekerera bza kuipa.
Tsapano, ndiri kukumbirani Mbuya kuti mundiphe. Bziri bwino kuti ine-pano ndife kuposa kukhala na moyo.”
Ndipo Mbuya adamubvunza kuti: “Kodi kukalipa koku n'khwa bwino?”
Ndipo iye adacoka mu m'zindamo aciyenda kukakhala kumabva dzuwa, ndipo kumweko adakonza cikumbi acikhala m'mwemo kuti adzaone n'ciani cingadadzacitika mu m'zindamo.
Mbuya adameresa m'tanga, uciyanga pa ntsodzi pa cikumbi ca Jona, kuti umucitire m'thunzi, umupepese ukali bwace. Pamwepo Jona adakondwa kwene-kwene, thangwe la m'tangayo.
Tsono mwangwana yanzace, Mulungu adatumiza cikonye cicikafukuta m'tagayo, iwo uciwumiratu.
Pomwe kudacena, Mulungu adacita dzuwa kwene-kwene, licimutentha Jona mum'solo mpaka iye acigwa cikomo. Ndipo iye adafunisisa kufa na m'tima wace wentse, acilewa kuti: “Bziri bwino kuti ine-pano ndife kuposa kukhala tenepano uno!”
Pamwepo Mulungu adamubvunza Jona kuti: “Kodi iwepo uli kukalipa na thangwe la m'tangayu?” Jona adatawira aciti: “Bziri bwino inde kukalipako, kuti ndife.”
Tsono Mbuya adalewa kuti: “Iwepo wabvera ntsisi m'tanga, omwe ulibe kuwubonerera na kuwukuza. Iwo udamera ntsiku ibodzi, mangwana yanzace uciwumiratu.
Niniva ni m'zinda ukulu kwene-kwene. Una wanthu bzulu dzana na makumi mawiri, omwe an'dziwa lini kuti boko la didi na la dzere ndiponi, na bzifuwo bzizinji pomwe. Ningaleke tani kuwubvera ntsisi?”




































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Kuyamba kwa Mafala Yabwino yakulewa bza Jezu Krixtu, Mwana wa Mulungu.
Ninga mpolofiti Isaya adanemba kuti:“Mulungu adati, Ndin'dzatuma mtumiki wangu kutsogolo kwako, kuti akakondze njira yomwe iwe udzapitembo.
Fala la munthu wakukuwa mthengo ali kulewa kuti, ‘Kondzani njira yakudzapitira Mbuya, thamulani miseu yomwe adzapitembo.’”
N'cadidi adawoneka Juwau M'batizi kuthengo acilalika, “Sandulikani mtima, mubatizidwe. Mulungu an'dzakulekererani bzakuipa bzanu.”
Akhabwera kwa iye wanthu wakucokera kumbali zentse za Judeya na Jerusalemu. Iwo akhazimbula bzakuipa bzawo, Juwau akhawabatiza mumkulo wa Jorodau.
Iye akhabvala khanda la nchefu, akhamanga mciuno na mceka. Cakudya cace cikhali mabombo na uci bwa mthengo.
Akhalalika aciti: “Pambuyo pangu pakubwera winango wamphambvu kuposa ine. Wakuti ine ndine wakusaya kufunika ngakhale kukotama kutsudzula thambo za xangu zace.
Ine ndakubatizani na madzi, tsono Iye an'dzakubatizani na Mzimu Wakucena.”
Ntsiku zimwezo Jezu adabwera kucokera kuNazalee, mui ubodzi wa Galileya, acibatiziwa na Juwau mumkulo wa Jorodau.
Pakucoka mmadzimo, adawona kudzulu kwakufunguka, ndipo Mzimu Wakucena udabuluka kwa Iye ninga nkhangaiwa.
Kudzulu kudabveka mafala yakuti: “Iwe ndiwe Mwana wangu wa pamtima. Nimbakomedwa nawe kwakukulu.”
Nthawe imweyo Mzimu Wakucena udapitisa Jezu mthengo.
Adakhala kumweko ntsiku makumi manai. Sathani adamuyeza. Bzikhalipombo bzirombo bza mthengo. Tsono anjo zikhamutumikira.
Ataikhidwa kaidi Juwau, Jezu adayenda kuGalileya acilalika Mafala yabwino yakulewa bza Mulungu.
Adati: “Nthawe yakwana. Bwafika Ufumu bwa Mulungu. Sandulikani mtima. Khulupirirani Mafala Yabwino.”
Pakuyenda mmphephete mwa thawale la Galileya, Jezu adawona wanthu awiri, Sirimau na m'bale wace Andereya, akhatheya bwazi mmadzi, thangwe akhali akhongwe.
Adawauza Jezu: “Imwe munditewere, ndikusanduseni akhongwe wa wanthu.”
Adasiyeratu mabwaziyo ndipo adamutewera.
Atafamba pang'ono, adawona Tiyagu na Juwau, wana wa Zebedeu, omwe akhali mmwadiya kukondza mabwazi.
Jezu adawacemera, ndipo adasiya baba wawo Zebedeu mmwadiya pabodzi na anyabasa wace, acitewera.
Adayenda wentse kuKafernau. Yatafika ntsiku ya malinkhuma, Jezu adayenda mnyumba ya mapembero, acipfundzisa.
Wentse adadabwa na bzakupfundzisa bzace thangwe akhapfundzisa na utongi, akhasiyana ninga amisiri wa Mtemo.
Nthawe pang'ono adawoneka mnyumba ya mapemberomo munthu wakuphatidwa na mzimu wakuipa. Adalewa na kukuwa aciti:
“Tina ciani na Imwe, Jezu wa Nazalee? Kodi mwabwera kudzatidzonga? Ndakudziwani kuti ndimwe Wakucena wa Mulungu.”
Ndipo Jezu adalamulira mzimu wakuipayo, aciti, “Khala zii, coka mwa munthuyu.”
Pamwepo mzimu wakuipa ule udamutekenyesa munthuyo kwakukulu ucikuwa kwene-kwene, ndipo udacoka.
Wentse wale adadabwa kwakukulu acimbabvundzana, “Kodi bzimwebzi n'ciani? Cakupfundzisa cipsa cimweci! Ambaitonga mizimu yakuipa na mphambvu, ndipo idamubvera.”
Mwakamkulumize, mbiri yace idamwazika mbali zentse za Galileya.
Pambuyo pace Jezu adacoka kunyumba ya mapembero kule, adayenda kunyumba ya Sirimau na Andereya pabodzi na Tiyagu na Juwau .
Mibzala wa Sirimau akhadagona kwakufesuka, pamwepo wanthu adawuza Jezu bza matendayo.
Jezu adayenda aciwaphata boko aciwamusa, ndipo maferu yadamala. Na tenepo mai ule adawaphikira cakudya.
Maulo, latamira dzuwa, adawabweresa wentse wanthu kwa Jezu wakuduwala na wakuphatidwa na mizimu yakuipa.
Wentse wa mumzindamu adagwezekana pamsuwo.
Jezu adalimbisa azinji omwe akhabonera na matenda yakusiyana-siyana, acicosa mizimu yakuipa, aciiletsa kulewa-lewa thangwe idamuzindikira.
Macibese-bese kukhanati kucena, Jezu adamuka aciyenda kuthengo. Kumweko adakapembera.
Sirimau na andzace adamunyang'ana mbali zentse.
Atamugumana adamuuza kuti: “Wanthu wentse ali kukunyang'anani.”
Tsono Iye adatawira kuti: “Mbatiyendeni tipite kumidzi inango pafupi na pam'pano, ndikalalike mafala kumweko. Thangwe ndibzo ndidabwerera.”
Ndipo adayenda acilalika mnyumba zentse za mapembero kuGalileya kwentseko acicosa mizimu yakuipa.
Munthu winango wa mapere adabwera kwa Jezu. Adagodama acimudandaulira: “Mucifuna, mungakwanise kundilimbisa.”
Jezu adamubvera ntsisi. Adatambalisa boko lace acimukhuya acilewa, “Cadidi, ndafuna, ulimbe!”
Panthawe ibodzi-bodziyo mapere yace yadamala, acicenesewa.
Ndipo Jezu adamuwuza kuti acoke acimucenjeza
kuti, “Uleke kuwuza ali-yentse bzimwebzi, tsono uyende ukabziwonese kwa azibaba wantsembe*, ukapereke ntsembe yomwe adalamula Mozeji ikakhale mboni kuti walimbadi.”
Adandocoka pamwepo, munthuyo adayamba kumbazimbula bzentse na kumwaza nkhani. Na tenepo bzikhafunika lini kuti Jezu awoneke padeca mmizinda mwentse tsono akhakhala kuthengo. Ndipo wanthu akhambayenda kwa Iye kucokera mbuto na mbuto.
Patapita ntsiku pang'ono, Jezu adabwera pomwe kuKafernau. Bzidabveka kuti ali kunyumba.
Azinji adagumana mnyumbamo. Ndipo angakhale na pamsuwo pakhalibe mbuto yakupitira. Jezu, pakulewa mafala ya Mulungu.
Wanthu anai adanyamula bundukutu aciyenda naye.
Alibe kufika pafupi na Jezu thangwe ra mthithi wa wanthu. Adakwira pantsodzi ya nyumba, acinyasula ntsodziyo kulinganiza pakhana Jezu. Ndipo adamubulusa bundukutu ule pamacira.
Pakuwona cikhulupiriro cawo, Jezu adawuza bundukutuyo kuti, “Mwana wangu, bzakuipa bzako bzalekereredwa.”
Tsono pamwepo wakhadakhalambo amisiri wa Mtemo wa Mozeji. Iwo adayamba kubzibvundza mumtima mwawo kuti,
“Kodi Umweyu angalewe tani tenepo? Kunyoza lini Mulungu kumweku? Mbani angalekerere bzakuipa? Ni Mulungu yekha!”
Ndipo Jezu mumzimu adadziwa kuti akhakumbuka bzimwebzi mumtima mwawo, na tenepo adawabvundza kuti, “Thangwe ranyi mun'kumbuka bzimwebzi mmitima mwanu?
Cakupusa n'ciponi, kumuwuza bundukutuyu kuti, ‘Bzakuipa bzako bzalekereredwa,’ ayai, ‘Muka, tenga macira yako, uyende?’
Tsono kuti mudziwe Mwana-wa-Munthu ali nayo mphambvu pantsi pano yakulekerera bzakuipa, wonani.” Ndipo adauza bundukutuyo,
“Iwe, muka, tenga macira yako, uyende kumui.”
Pamaso pawentse, munthu ule adamuka, acitenga macira yace acicoka. Wanthu wentse adadabwa kwene-kwene, acipasa mbiri Mulungu acimbalewa, “Cipo bzimwebzi tikanati kubziwona.”
Jezu adayenda pomwe kugombe. Wanthu azinji adafika kumweko, ndipo Iye adawapfundzisa.
Pakufamba Jezu, adawona Levi, mwana wa Alifeu, akhadakhala pambuto ya basa la msonkho. Adamuuza aciti, “Iwe, unditewere.” Ndipo adamuka acimutewera.
Pomwe Jezu akhadya mnyumba mwa Levi, pakhana wanthu azinji wakupimisa msonkho na wanthu wakuphonya. Akhadya na Jezuyo pabodzi na wakupfundzira wace. Thangwe akhalipo azinji wa iwo omwe akhatewera iye.
Pakhali amisiri wa Mtemo wa Afaliseyu ndipo adawona kuti Jezu an'kudya na wanthu wakuphonya na wanthu wakupimisa msonkho, adabvundza wakupfundzira wace kuti, “Thangwe ranyi an'kudya pabodzi na wakupimisa msonkho na wanthu wakuphonya?”
Jezu adabva bzimwebzo adawatawira kuti, “Wanthu omwe mbakulimba an'nyangana lini mulapi. Wakuduwala ndiye an'nyangana mulapi! Ine ndiribe kubwera kudzacemera wanthu wakulungama, tsono ndabwera kudzacemera wakuphonya.”
Tsapano wakupfundzira wa Juwau M'batizi na Afaliseyu akhabzimana kudya. Wanthu adabwera kwa Jezu acimbabvundza aciti, “Wakupfundzira wa Juwau na wakupfundzira wa Afaliseyu ambabzimana kudya. Thangwe ranyi wakupfundzira wanu ambabzimana lini?”
Jezu adatawira, “Kodi andzace wa mwenekaciro msinda ya malowozi angasale kudya pomwe namwaliyo ali nawo? Bzingacitike lini! Iwo angasale lini kudya pomwe namwaliyo ali nawo.
Tsono in'dzafika nthawe yomwe an'dzawacosera namwaliyo. Nthawe imweyo an'dzabzimana kudya.”
“Palibe angasonere cakubvala ca kale na cigamba cipsa. Thangwe angacita tenepo, cigamba cire cimbanyothokera cicikuza mubo. Ndipo kung'ambika kwace kumbakhala kwakukulu kusiyana kale.
Ndipombo munthu angathire lini vinyu ipsa mmabudu ya khanda la kale. Thangwe angacita tenepo, mabudu yambang'ambika, ndipo vinyu ire imbataika. Mabuduyo nkhumala basa. Tsono bzin'funika kuikha vinyu mmabudu yapsa.”
Pantsiku inango ya malinkhuma, Jezu akhapita mminda ya tirigu. Akhayenda tenepo, wakupfundzira wace adayamba kucosa ngala za tirigu acimbadya.
Pamwepo Afaliseyu adabvundza Jezu kuti, “Thangwe ranyi wakupfundira wanu ali kucita bzomwe bzin'funika lini pantsiku ya malinkhuma?”
Iye adatawira, “Thangwe ranyi mun'cita ninga mulibe kuwerenga bzomwe adacita David na andzace, pomwe wakhana njala?
Iye adapita mnyumba ya Mulungu, panthawe yomwe Abiyatali akhali mkulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe, acikadya mkate wakuperekedwa kwa Mulungu? Na tenepo mkate umweyo ukhali wakuletsedwa kuti winango ali-wentse adye, kupambula azibaba wa ntsembe wokha. Tsono adagawirambo andzace wale omwe akhali naye.”
Ndipo Jezu pakupitiriza fala, adauza Afaliseyuwo kuti, “Mulungu adaikha ntsiku ya malinkhuma kuti ikhale yakuthandiza wanthu. Alibe kulenga wanthu kuti akhale akapolo wa ntsiku ya malinkhuma.
Na tenepo Mwana-wa-Munthu ana mphambvu ngakhale kwa ntsiku ya malinkhuma.”
Jezu adapita pomwe mnyumba yamapemphero. Momwemo mukhana munthu winango wakupunduka boko.
Wanthu winango akhanyangana thangwe ra kupasira mulandu Jezuyo, na tenepo akhanyang'anisa kuti aone angamulimbise munthuyo pa ntsiku ya kupuma.
Jezu adawuza munthu wakupundaka boko ule kuti, “Ima, bwera kutsogolo kuno.”
Ndipo adabvundza wanthu wale kuti, “Kodi pa ntsiku ya malikhuma cin'bvumizidwa n'ciponi? Kucita bzabwino, ayai kucita bzakuipa? Kupulumusa moyo wa munthu, ayai kuudzonga?” Wanthuwo adakhala zii.
Jezu pakuo kuti wakhada wuma ndzelu mtima wace udamuwawa, pakuwona kuti akhali wanthu wamakani tenepo, ndipo adawayang'ana na ukali. Ndipo adamuwuza munthuyo kuti, “Thamula boko lako.” Iye adalithamula, ndipo boko lacero lidakhalambo bwino.
Pamwepo Afaliseyeu wale adacoka adakagumanizana na wanthu wa phati ra Herodi, kuti apangane njira yakuphera Jezu.
Jezu pabodzi na wakupfundzira wace adacoka pompale acienda kugombe la Galileya. Mthithi ukulu wa wanthu udamutewera.
Wanthu wale akhali wa ku Galileya, winango wa ku Judeya na ku Jerusalemu, winango wa ku Idumeya, na wang'ambo wa kumkulo wa Jorodau, ndipombo kucipande ca ku Tiru na Sidoni. Wentsenewo adafika kwa Iye, thangwe wakhabva bzizinji bzomwe Iye akhacita.
Jezu adauza wakupfundzira wace kuti amuikire mwadiya pafupi, akha gopesa kuti wanthu angayambe kum'psinyiza, thangwe ukhali mthithi ukulu
Na kuona kuti akhaciza wanthu azinji, ndipopo wentse omwe akhana matenda akhambagwinyana-gwinyana pakufuna kuti am'khuye.
Pomwe mizimu yakuipa ikamuwona ikhabzigwesa pantsi kutsogolo kwa Iye icimbakuwa kuti, “Imwe ndimwe Mwana wa Mulungu.”
tsono Iye akhambailetsa mwa mphambvu kuti ileke kumuzimbula.

Pamwepo adasankhula kumi na awiri, aciwacemera dzina la kuti, “Atumiki.” Adawauza kuti, “ndasakhula imwe kuti mumbakhale na ine, ndin'dzakutumani kukalalika,
dicikupasani mphambvu yakuthotha mizimu yakuipa.”
Wanthu kumi na awiri omwe adasankhuliwa mbawa: Sirimau (omwe Jezu adamucemera Pedru),
Tiyagu na m'bale wace Juwau, wana wa Zebedeu (omwewo adawapasa dzina linango lakuti Aboanerje, bziri kulewa kuti “Wakugopswa ninga Wana wa Ciphaliwali”)87,
Andereya, Filipe, Bartolomeyu, Mateyu, Tomasi, Tiyagu (mwana wa Alifeu), Tadeyu, Sirimau (wa phati landale la Azelote,)
ndipombo Judasi Iskaliote (omwe adapereka Jezu.)
Pambuyo pace Jezu adaenda kunyumba, ndipo wanthu azinji adagumana pomwe, na tenepo Iye na wakupfundzira wace alibe kudzaone nthawe ya kuti adye.
Abale wace na kubva bzimwebzi, adabwera kuti adzamutenge, thangwe iwo akhati, “Ali kucita nsala.”
Amisiri winango wa Mtemo, omwe adabwera kucokera ku Jerusalemu, akhalewa kuti, “Munthu omweyu waphatidwa na Belezebu*.”Akhalewa pomwe, “Mphambvu zomwe umweyu ambacosera mizimu yakuipa nzakucokera kwa mkulu wa mizimuyo.”
Na tenepo Jezu adacemera wanthu kuti abwere pafupi, aciwauza na mifanilizo kuti, “Nandi Satana angabzithothe yekha?
Wanthu wa mu umambo uli-wentse angayamba kusandukirana, umambo umwewo bunipitiriza lini .
Ndipo pomwe wanthu wa mbanja libodzi angayamba kugawika, banja limwero limpitiriza lini.
Na tenepo penu mu umambo wa Satana ngwakusandukirana na kupambulana, na tenepoyo bwamala.
“palibe omwe angakwanise kupita mnyumba ya munthu wamphambvu acimubera bzinthu bzace akanati kum'manga. na tenepo ambatoma kum'manga acimubera bwino.
“Ncadidi ndiri kulewa kuti wanthu angakwanise kulekereredwa bzakuipa bzentse, napo bzakulewa bzawo bzentse bzicikhala bzakunyoza Mulungu.
Tsono ali-yentse wakunyoza Mzimu Wakucena, an'dzalekereredwa lini bzakuipa bzace bzimbakhala bza kuyenda na kuyenda thagwe ni kaidi wa bzakuipa bzakusaya kumala .”
Jezu adalewa bzimwebzi pakuwona kuti wanthu wale akhalewa kuti, “Waphatidwa na mzimu wakuipa.”
Mai na abale wace Jezu adabwera kumuiko. Adaima panja, adatuma wanthu kuti akamucemere.
Wanthu azinji akhadakhala acimuzungulira. Ndipo wale adamuuza kuti, “Mai wako na abale wako ali panjapa, ali kukucemera.”
Tsono Iye adati, “Mai wangu! Abale wangu! Waponi pomwe?”
Pamwepo adayang'ana wanthu wale omwe akhadakhala acimuzungulira aciti, “Ine mai wangu na abale wangu mbawa.
Ali-yentse omwe ancita bzomwe Mulungu an'funa, womwewo ndiwo am'bale wangu, na mai wangu.”

Tsono kufuna-funa bza pantsi-pano, kufunisisa nthaka na kusirira bzinthu bzinango bzizinji bzimbapitambo nkhusayisa mphambvu mafala yale, na tenepo yambadzabereka lini bzisapo.
ndipo mbeu zakubzalidwa pa mataka yabwino bziri kulewa wanthu omwe wambabva mafala ya Mulungu, waciyatambira. wacibereka bzisapo, yinango makumi matatu, yinango makumi matanthatu, yinango dzana.”
Tsono Jezu adawabvundza kuti, “Kodi wanthu ambatenga lampalina acigwanankira na mtsuko, ayai kuibisa mfunfuntsi mwa talimba? Ambaikha lini padeca?
Na tenepo ciri-centse cakubisika cin'dzaoneka, pomwe ciri-centse ca kabise-bise bzin'dzazimbuka padeca.
Ule ana makutu yakubva, abve!”
Adawauza pomwe kuti, “Mumbakhale na tcero na mafala yomwe mumbabva. [maphatidwe uncita winango] Mulungu an'dzaphatisambo basa cibodzibodzico pakuweruzambo imwepo, na tenepo kwa imwepo an'dzathimizira.
Pamwepo omwe ana cinthu kale, an'dzamuthimizira cinango. Tsono omwe alibe cinthu, cing'ono comwe anaco an'dzamutengera basi.”
Jezu adalewa pomwe kuti, Umambo bwa Mulungu tingandendemeze na munthu wakubzala mbeu mmunda.
Omwe ambandogona usiku na masikati, nthawe yentseneyo mbeu yomwe adabzala ire idamera icikula, mwenekaciroyo ne kudziwa momwe bziri kucitikira.
Pamwepo mataka yambaberekesa pomwe mbeu ire yokha-yokha. ambayamba ni nyakamera, zicibwera ngala-ngala, pambuyo pace bzisapo mungala-ngala mule bzimbakhuma.
Tsono bzisapo bzingacena, munthu ule ambatenga cisu nkhumbagwata, thangwe nthawe yakubvuna yakwana.”
Jezu adabvunza pomwe, “Kodi Umambo bwa Mulungu tingaundendemeze na ciyani? Ayai tiufananize na ciyani?
Udakhala ninga mbeu ya mtowe. Ingabzaliwa njing'ono kwene-kwene kuposa mbeu zinango pantsi pano.

Jezu akhalewa nawo na mifananizo mizinji ninga imwei, pakundendemeza na ndzeru za wanthuwo.
akhalewa lini acisaya kuwapasa mifananizo. Tsono akhati akakhala payekha na wakupfundzira wace, akhambawafokotozera bzentse.

Jezu na wakupfundzira wace adafika ng'ambu ya Thawale la Galileya, mbali ya Gerasa.
Pomwe iye adandocoka mmwadiya, padabwera munthu winango wakuphatidwa na mzimu wakuipa acicokera ku thenje.

kazinji wanthu akhamba m'manga miyendo na waya, ndipombo kum'manga manja na cingwe, tsono iye akhambabwedza unyolo bule, ndipo waya zakumanga miyendozo akhambagwata. Pakhalibe na m'bodziyo omwe akhakwanisa kumukunda.
Masikati na usiku akhambakhala kuthenjeko na mmapiri, acimbandokuwa na kubzipweteka na minyala.

akhalewa terepo thangwe Jezu akhadalewa kuti, “Mzimu wakuipawe, coka mwa munthuyu!”

omwe adaona bzentse wale, adawafotokozera bzomwe bzidacitika kwa munthu ule na kwa nkhumba zire.

Ndipo alibe kubvumiza kuti winango amutewere iye, kupambula Pedru, na Tiyagu, na Juwau, m'bale wa Tiyaguyo.
Pomwe iwo adafika kunyumba kwa mkulu ule wa nyumba yamapemphero Jezu adaona phiringo la wanthu omwe, ali akhalira acimbakuwa.
Iye adapita, aciwabvundza kuti, “Thangwe ranyi muli kucita phiringu na kukuwa Mwanayu alibe kufa adandogona .”
Pamwepo wanthuwo adayamba kumuseka.iye adawacosa panja wentse, acitenga baba na mai wa mwanayo, na omwe akhali naye wale, acipita kucipinda kukhana mwana ule.
Ndipo adaphata boko la mwanayo acimuuza kuti, “Talita, kumi.” (Ndiko kulewa kuti, “Mtsikana-we, ndiri kukuuza kuti muka.”)
mthawe ibodzi-bodziyo mtsikanayo adamukadi, aciyamba kufamba. iye akhana magole khumi na mawiri. Pamwepo wanthu wale adadabwa kwene-kwene.
Tsono Jezu adawalamula mwa mphambvu kuti bzimwebzi winango ali-yentse aleke kubzidziwa. aciwauza kuti am'pase cakudya mtsikana ule.
Jezu adacoka kumweko, acikafika kumui kwace pabodzi na wakupfunzdzira wace.
Pomwe idafika ntsiku ya malinkhuma, Iye adayamba kupfundzisa mnyumba yamapemphero. Wanthu azinji omwe akhamutetekera adadabwa kwene-kwene acimbalewa kuti, “Kodi mamuna umweyu adabzipfunzdira kuponi bzentsenebzi? Udziwi bumwebu adabuwona kuponi? An'kwanisa tani kucita bzidabwiso tenepayu?
Kodi omweyu ndiye lini misiri wa matabwa ule, mwana wa Maliya? Kodi abale wace ndiwo lini Tiyagu, na Zuze, na Judasi, na Sirimau? Ndiye lini omwe ana mfuma-kazi tinazozi?” Na tenepo alibe kufuna kudzadziwa pomwe bza iye .
Tsono Jezu adawauza kuti, “Mpolofiti ambalemekezedwa kumbuto zinango, kupambula kumui kwawo, pakati pa abale wace, ndipombo kunyumba kwawo.”
Na tenepo angadacita lini bzidabwiso kumweko. Adandosanzika manja kwa wakuduwala ang'ono-ng'ono, aciwalimbisa.
pamwepo iye adadabwa pakuwona kuti wanthu wakumweko alibe kukhulupirira. Pambuyo pace Jezu adayenda ku mii ya mmphepete, acimbapfundzisa wanthu.
Jezu adacemera wakupfundzira wace khumi na awiri aciwatuma awiri-awiri. Aciwapasa mphambvu yakucosera mizimu yakuipa
Aciwalamula kuti, “pakuenda lekani kutenga cinthu ciri-centse, kupambula mpsimbo yokha. Lekani kutenga cakudya, ayai gumbu lakufamba nalo, ayai kobiri mukabudu.

Penu kumbuto kwinango wanthu an'kutambirani lini, acilamba kubva mafala yanu, pakucoka kwanu mukunkhumule pfumbi la minyendo yanu. Cimweci cin'dzakhala cizindikiro cakuti wa-na mulandu.”
Tsono wakupfundzira wale adayenda, acimbalalikira wanthu kuti asandulike mtima.
Akhacosa mizimu yakuipa mizinji, ndipombo acimbadzoza mafuta wanthu wakudwala azinji acimbawalimbisa.
Mambo Herodi akhadabzibva bzimwebzi, thangwe mbiri ya Jezu likhadabveka kwentse-kwentse. Wanthu winango akhati, “Juwau M'batizi adamuka kwa wakufa, ndipopa ali kucita bzidabwiso bzentsenebzi.”
Tsono winango akhati, “Ayai, omweyu ni Eliya.” winango akhati, “Uyu ni mpolofiti ninga m'bodzi wa apolofiti wakale.”
Pomwe Herodi adabva bzomwebzo, adati, “Adamuka kwa wakufa ule, ni Juwau omwe ndidagwata khosi.”
Thangwe Herodiyo kale adatuma acikunda wace kuti akam'phate Juwau, akam'mange acithusa m'kaidi. Adacita bzimwebzire thangwe ra Herodiasi, m'kazi wa Filipe, m'bale wace. na kuti Herodi akhadamulowola m'kaziyo.
Ndipo Juwau akhambamuuza kuti, “Nkhuponya Mtemo kupsokhonyola m'kazi wa m'bale wanu.”
ndipo Herodiasi akhambawenga Juwau, na tenepopo akhafuna kuti amuphe. Tsono akhataza,
thangwe Herodi akhambamgopa Juwau, pakudziwa kuti akhali munthu wakulungama acilungama. ndipopo akhamkoya bwino. Akhafuna kumbabva mafala yace, ngakhale kuti akumubva tenepo, akhamala ndzeru naye.
Tsono pa ntsiku yakukondwerera kubadwa kwa Herodi, Herodiasi adawona mphata. Herodi ule adakondza uzokoto, acicemera akulu-akulu wa Boma, na akulu wakutonga acikunda, na atongi wa ku Galileya.
Ndipo mwana wacikazi wa Herodiasi adapita, aciyamba kubzina.herodi na wakucemeredwa wale adakomedwa Kwene-kwene nakubzina kule. Pamwepo mambo adauza mtsikana ule kuti, “Undikumbire ciri-centse comwe un'funa, ine ninkupasa.”
Na tenepo adalumbira aciti, “Ciri-centse comwe undikumbira, ninkupasa, ngakhale cipande ca umambo bwangu.”
Mtsikanayo adacoka acikabvundza mai wace kuti, “Kodi ndikakumbire ciyani?” Mai wace adati “Kakumbire msolo wa Juwau M'batizi.”
Ndipo Mtsikana ule adabwerera mwa kankulumize kwa mambo acimuuza kuti, “nifuna kuti tsapanopa mundipase msolo wa Juwau M'batizi mphande!”
Na tenepo mambo Herodi adabva ntsisi kwene-kwene. Tsono thangwe ra kulumbira komwe akhadacita patsogolo pa wakucemeredwa, mambo akhafuna lini kupfudza cipangano comwe adacita na mtsikana ule.
mwakamkulumize adatuma m'bodzi wa acikunda wace, kuti abwerese msolo wa Juwau. ncikunda ule adayenda ku kaidi, acikagwata msolo wa Juwau.
Adauikha mphande acidzaupereka kwa mtsikana ule, mtsikanayo nkhukauperekambo kwa mai wace.
Wakupfundzira wa Juwau pomwe adabva bzimwebzo, adabwera acidzatenga nkhawa ire acikapendesa mucigwindza kuthenje.
Atumiki adabwerera kwa Jezu acimufotokozera bzentse bzomwe adacita na kupfundzisidwa.
Jezu adawauza kuti “Mbatiyendeni kumbuto imbapita lini wanthu, kuti mukapume pang'ono.” Adalewa terepo thangwe wanthu akhali nyalu-nyalu, nakuti iwo akhalibe phata wa kuti angada'kwanisa kudya
cadidi iwo adapita mmwadiya acienda okha kumbuto komwe kukhalibe wanthu
Tsono wanthu azinji adawaona pakucoka, aciwazindikira. Na tenepo adathamanga na n'gambo ire kucokera ku mizinda yentse, acitoma kufika, Jezu na wakupfundzira wace wale akhanati kufika.
Pamwe Jezu adacoka mmwadiya, adaona mthithi ukulu wa wanthu. Adawabvera ntsisi, thangwe wakhali ninga mabira yakusaya makabusa, na tenepo adayamba kuwapfundzisa bzizinji.
Nthawe ya kumaulo wakupfundzira wace adadzamuuza kuti, “Kuno nkhuthengo, ndipo kwadoka
Auzeni wanthuwa wayende, wakadye m'mii yomwe iri pafupiyi kuti akagule cakudya.”
Tsono Jezu adawauza kuti, “Imwepo apaseni cakudya.” Iwo adati, “tsono kuti wakwane wathuwa, pafunika kuti tikagule mkate wa kobiri za parata zikwanira madzana mawiri kuti tidzawadyese wentsewa!”
Na tenepo Jezu adawabvundza kuti, “Muna mikate mingasi? Ndokoni mukaone.” Adayenda kukaona ndipo adati, “Iripo mikate mixanu na ntsomba ziwiri.”
Ndipo Jezu adawawuza kuti, wentse wakhale pantsi kabugwe-kabugwe pakapinga.
Cadidi wanthu wale wadakhala pantsi, bungwe linango wanthu dzana, linango wanthu makumi maxanu.
Jezu adatenga mikate mixanu ire na ntsomba ziwiri zire, aciyang'ana kudzulu, acitenda Mulungu. Tsapano adayamba kugwata-gwata mikate ire, na ntsomba ziwiri acinjedza-njedza acipereka kwa wakupfundzira wace kuti wagawire wanthu wale.
Wanthu wentse adadya mpaka kukhuta.
Pambuyo pace wakupfundzira wale, wadatewnga mikate yakusala na ntsomba zire acidzaza madengu khumi na mawiri.
wanthu omwe adadya mikate ire kuwerenga amuna okha akhakwana bzulu bzixanu.
Watandomala, Jezu adawauza wakupfundzira wace kuti wapite mmwadiya, watsogole kuyenda n'gambuire ya Betsaida, Iye akhamba ngonekambo nthiti ule wa wanthu kuti wayende kwawo.
pomwe adagonekana nawo, adakwira ku phiri kukapemphera.
pomwe kukhayamba kudoka, mwadiya ule ukhali pakati nakati ya nyadza, Jezu akhali yekha kunja.
Ndipo adaona wakupfundzira wale akhacapa mwakuneseka, thangwe akhayenda kukhacokera condzi.yomweyo ikhali nthawe ya Madandakweca, Jezu adafamba padzulu pa madzi aciyenda kuna iwo acicita ninga an'funa kuwapitirira.
Tsono wakupfundzira wale, pakumuwona acifamba padzulu pa madzi, adakumbuka kuti nciphoko, adayamba kukuwa,
nakuti wentse pakumuona wadakhala na mantha. Tsono nthawe yomweyo Jezu adawauza kuti, “limbikani mtima ndine, lekani kugopa.”
Pamwepo iye adapita mmwadiya momwe iwo akhali, ndipo codzi cidaleka. Iwo adamalidwa ndzeru
thangwe alibe kubvesesa bwino bza kutupisidwa kwa mikate ire.thangwe akhalibe nabzo thupo.
Jezu na wakupfundzira wace adayambuka gombe, acifika ku Genesalee, acitsamisa mwadiya pagombe.
Pomwe iwo adandocoka mmwadiya, mbumba idamuzindikira Jezu.
wadathamangira ku mbuto zentse za mbali ire, aciyamba kumbabwera na wanthu wakuduwala pa macira, kumbuto komwe akhabva kuti Jezu ali uku.
Kuli-kwentse komwe Jezu akhayenda, ku mii na ku mizinda, wanthu akhadzakhazika wakudwala mmisika. Acimukumbira kuti abvumize wakuduwalayo kuphata ayai kondomukhuya bzakubvala bzace. Nakuti wentse omwe akhakhuya, akhalimba.
Afaliseyu winango pabodzi na apfundzisi winango wa Mtemo, omwe adacokera ku Jerusalemu, adasonkhana m'uphepete mwa Jezu.
Iwo wadawona kuti wakupfundzira wace winango wakhambadya cakudya na mmanja mwakuswipa (ndiye kuti wakhalibe kuteweza mtemo wa kusamba mmanja ninga momwe wafalizeyu wakhadayiwuza mbumba kuti yicite.)
Thangwe Afaliseyu na Ajuda wentse ambadya lini alibe kusamba mmanja na tcero, kuti akoye mtemo wa makolo.
Ndipo angacoka ku msika, ambadya lini wakanati kubzitsuka bzetse bzomwe wabweranabzo. Ambakoya pomwe mitemo inango mizinji yomwe makolo yawo yadawasiyira, ninga kutsuka mikhombo, bzikhalango, na bzikasi bza mkuwa [na talimba.]
Na tenepo Afaliseyu na amisiri wa Mtemo wale wadabvundza Jezu kuti, “Thangwe ranyi wakupfundzira wanu ambakoya lini mtemo wa makolo, tsono ambandodya napo alibe kusamba mmanja?”
Jezu adawatawira kuti, “Imwe wanthu wa ciphamaso, ncadidi bzomwe mpolofiti Isaya adalewa pa cipande caimwe, iye adanemba kuti, ‘Wanthuwa ambandondilemekeza na mulomo basi, tsono mitima yawo iri kutali na Ine.
kundipemba kwawo nkhwakusaya basa, thangwe wambapfundzisa mitemo ya wanthu, ninga walikuphundzisa mitemo ya mulungu.’”
Jezu adapitiriza, “Imwe mumbasiya Mtemo wa Mulungu, mucimbakoya mitemo ya wanthu.”
Tsono pakupitiriza mafala, Jezu adati, “Tsono imwe muna njira yanu yakucenjera yakusiyira Mtemo wa Mulungu kuti mukoye mitemo yanu.
Nakuti Mozeji adalewa kuti, ‘Lemekeza Baba wako na mai wako,’ ndipombo kuti, ‘Wakunyoza Baba wace ayai mai wace, aphewe.’
Tsono imwe mumbati, ‘Munthu akawuza Baba wace ayai mai wace kuti, “Bzomwe ndingadakuthandizani nabzo ndabzipereka kuna Mulungu, ”
umweyo anfunika lini pomwe kuwathandiza Baba wace na mai wace.’
Na tenepo mafala ya Mulungu imwe mumbayasandusa yapezi, thangwe ra mtemo wanu omwe mumbasiyirana. Ndipo mumbacita bzinango bzizinji tenepayu.”
Pambuyo pace Jezu adacemera pomwe mthithi wa wanthu ule kuti ubwere, aciti: “Tetekerani mwentsenemwe, ndipo mubvesese.
bzentse bzomwe bzicoka kunja bzicipita mkati mwa munthu bzinimuswipisa lini. Tsono bzomwe bzimbacoka mwa iye ndibzo bzinimuswipisa.”
[“Omwe ana makutu yakubva, abve!”]
Pomwe Jezu adasiya mthithi ule wa wanthu acipita mnyumba, wakupfundzira wace wadamubvundza bza mfananizo ule.
Iye adati: “Kodi na imwembo mulikukhala ninga wanango wale; muli kubvesesa lini? Kodi muli kudziwa lini kuti bzetse bzakucokera kunja, na kupita mwa munthu, bzin'kwanisa lini kumuswipisa?
Thangwe bzin'pita lini mumtima mwace, tsono mmimba, pambuyo pace nkhukabzitaya ku thengo.” (Pakulewa bzimwebzi, Jezu adalamulira kuti bzakudya bzentse wanthu angakwanise kudya.)
Adati pomwe, “Bzomwe dzimbaswipisa munthu nidzire bzincoka mmtima mwace.
Thangwe mkati mwa mitima wa wanthu ndimo mumbacoka ndzeru zakuipa, za ciwerewere, za kuba, za kuphana,
upombo, kusirira, kuipa mtima, cinyengo, bzakunyantsa, kuipidwa, kunyoza, kubzikuza, ndipombo kupusa.
Bzakuipa bzentsenebzi bzimbacokera mkati mwa munthu, ndipo ndibzo bzimbamuswipisa.”
Jezu adanyamuka komweko aciyenda kumbali ya ku Tiru. adapita munyumba inango, ndipo akhafuna lini kuti wanthu wadziwe kuti iye ali kumweko. Tsono alibe kukwanisa kubisika,
Nakuti mkazi winango, omwe mwana wace wacikazi akhabonera na mzimu wakuipa, adabva bza Iye. Adabwera kwa Jezu acigodama kuminyendo kwace.
Mkaziyo akhali wakunja, wa dziko la Siro-Fenisiya. Adakumbira Jezu kuti akacose mzimu wakuipa kwa mwana wace.
Tsono Jezu adamutawira kuti, “ayai, alekeni wana atome adya acikhuta. Mpsabwino lini kutenga cakudya ca wana nkhuthusira tuntsidza.”
Pamwepo mkazi ule adati, “Ncadidi, Mbuya, tsono tuntsidza tumbakhala pafupi na mbuto yakudyera tucimbadya tumisuwa tomwe wana ambataya.”
Pamwepo Jezu adamuuza kuti, “Thangwe la matawiridwe yako, ndoko, mzimu wakuipa wacoka mwa mwana wako.”
pomwe mkazi ule adabwerera kunyumba kwace, adakawona mwana ule adagona pa talimba, mzimu wakuipa ule wacoka.
Jezu adacoka pomwe ku mbali ire ya ku Tiru, acipita na ku Sidoni, kuyenda ku thawale la ku Galileya, adapita na pakati pa Mizinda Khumi.
Wanthu winango wadamubweresera munthu omwe akhali mkhutwi na ubewewe. Wanthuwo adakumbira Jezu kuti amulimbise pakumsandzika manja munthu ule.
Jezu adamucosa munthu ule pa mthithi wa wanthu acienda naye pa mbali. Adapitisa bzala mmakutu mwace, acipsipa mata, nkhukuya lirime lace munthu ule.
Iye adanyang'ana kudzulu, acisisimira, acimuwuza kuti, “Efata!” ndiko kulewa “Funguka!”
makutu ya munthu ule adafunguka, pamwepo lirime lace lidatsudzuka, aciyamba kulewa-lewa bwino
Jezu adalumurira andzace wa munthu ule kuti, “Lekani kukawuza winango ali-yentse bzimwebzi.” Tsono napo iye akhadawaletsa, iwo adayenda acibzizimbula kwene-kwene.
Ndipo wanthu wentse omwe wakhabzibva wakhadabwa kwene-kwene. waciti, “Omweyu ambacita bzentse mbzabwino. Ngakhale mkhutwi ambazilimbisa zicibva, pomwe wakusaya kulewa-lewa ambawacitisa kuti walewe-lewe.”
Ntsiku inango, mthithi ukuru wa wanthu udagumana pomwe.nakuona kuti palibe cakudya, Jezu adacemera wakupfundzira wace aciwawuza kuti,
“Ndiri kuwabvera ntsisi wanthuwa, thangwe akhala nande ntsiku zitatu ndipo alibe cakudya.
Ningawabweza kwawo na njala tenepa, an'dzakomoka pa njira, thangwe winango acokera kutali.”
Wakupfundzira wace adamubvundza kuti, “Wanthu azinji terepayu munthu angawanyang'anire tani cakudya cakukwanira, munthuku muno?”
Jezu adawabvundza kuti, “Muna mikate mingasi?” Iwo wadatawira, “Minomwe.”
Pamwepo Jezu adauza mbumba ire kuti ikhale pantsi. Pambuyo pace adatenga mikate minomwe ire, acitenda Mulungu, adaigwatagwata aciipereka kwa wakupfundzira wace kuti agawire mbumba ire. Wakupfundzira wale wadaigawira mbumba ire.
Akhana tuntsomba pomwe tung'ono-ng'ono. Jezu adatenda Mulungu, acilamula wakupfundzira wace kuti agawire mbumba ire.
Wentse adadya acikhuta. Wadakokhobza bzakusala, acidzaza bzitundu bzinomwe.
Wanthu omwe akhali pamwepo, amuna okha akhali pafupi-fupi bzulu bzinai. Jezu adadzauza mbumba kuti iyende.
Pambuyo pace Iye na wakupfundzira wace adapita mmwadiya aciyenda ku mbali ya Dalammanuta.
Ndipo Afaliseyu wadaenda kuna Jezu, ku katsutsana naye. Iwo adamukumbira kuti awawonese cizindikiro cakudabwisa cakucokera kudzulu. Akhandofuna kumuteyera msampha basi.
Jezu adasisimira mu mtima aciti, “Thangwe ranyi wanthu wa tsapano lino wambafuna kuwona cizindikiro cakudabwisa? Ncadidi ndiri kulewa kuti palibe cizindikiro cidza citika kwa mbumba iyi.”
Na tenepo, adawasiya, acipita pomwe mmwadiya aciyambuka ng'ambu ire.
Pakucoka wakupfundzira wa Jezu akhadayebwa kutenga mkate, tsono mmwadiyamo akhana mkate ubodzi wokha.
Ndipo Jezu adawabebesa aciti, “Bvesesani mucenjere na cakutupisa ca wafaliseyu na ca Herodi.”
Pamwepo wakupfundzira wale adayamba kutsutsana acimbati, “Ali kulewa bzimwebzi thangwe tiribe mkate.”
Jezu adabva bzomwe iwo akhalewa. aciwabvundza kuti, “Thangwe ranyi muli kutsutsana kuti mulibe mkate? Kodi mukhanati kuzindikira ayai kubvesesa? Kodi misolo yanu njakuuma, nandi?
Maso munayo, tsono muniwona lini? Ndipo makutu munayo, tsono mumbabvesesa lini? kodi imwe m'nkubukira lini?
Pale ndidagwata-gwata mikate mixanu kuti ndidyese wanthu bzulu bzixanu, kodi mudadzaza bzitundu bzingasi bza bzakusala?” Wakupfundzira wale adati, “Bzitundu khumi na bziwiri.”
Jezu adawabvundza pomwe kuti, “Kodi pale ndidagwata-gwata mikate minomwe na kudyesa wanthu bzulu bzinai, mudakonkhobza bzitundu bzingasi bza bzakusala?” Iwo adati, “Bzitundu bzinomwe.”
Pamwepo Jezu adati, “Kodi mukanati kubva basi?”
Jezu na wakupfundzira wace adafika ku Betsaida. Kumweko wanthu adabwera na zimola, wacimukumbira kuti amukhuye.
Jezu adam'phata boko, acicoka naye kunja kwa mui. Adaikha mata mmaso mwa munthu ule, acimuikha boko acimubvundza kuti, “Kodi uli kuwona cinthu?”
Munthu ule adakwiza maso acilewa, “Ndiri kuwona wanthu ali kufamba-famba, tsono wali kuwoneka ninga miti.”
Adamuikha pomwe boko mmaso mwace. ndipo adapenya acipora, aciyamba kuwona bwino-bwino
Jezu adamuuza kuti ayende kwawo, acimuwuza kuti, “Uleke kubwerera ku mui ule.”
Jezu na wakupfundzira wace adayenda ku mii ya ku Sesaleya-Filipi. mu njira adabvundza wakupfundzira wace kuti, “Kodi wanthu ambalewa Ine ndine yani?”
Iwo adatawira kuti, “Winango ambalewa ndimwe Juwau M'batizi, winango ndimwe Eliya, winangombo ambalewa ndimwe m'bodzi wa apolofita.”
Pamwepo Jezu adawabvundza kuti, “Kodi imwepo, mumbati ndine yani?” Pedru adamutawira kuti, “Imwe ndimwe[kirixtu] Mpulumusi adalewedwa ule.”
Tsono Jezu adawalamula kuti waleke kuwuza munthu winango ali-yentse bza Iye.
Jezu adayamba kupfundzisa wakupfundzira wace kuti, “Mwana-wa-Munthu bzin'dzafunika kuti aboneresedwe kwene-kwene. Akulu wa Ayuda, na akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe na amisiri wa Mtemo wacidzamulamba. Iye an'dzaphedwa, tsono zingadzapita ntsiku zitatu an'dzamuka.”
Bzimwebzi adabzilewa padeca Na tenepo Pedru adamutenga aciyenda naye pambali, aciyamba kumutsimula.
Tsono Jezu adaceuka, acinyang'ana wakupfundzira wace winango wale, ndipo adatsimula Pedru. Adati, “Coka kwa ine, iwe Satana! Ndzeru yako ndiyo lini ndzeru ya Mulungu, ni ndzeru ya wanthu.”
Pambuyo pace Jezu adacemera mthithi wa wanthu pabodzi na wakupfundzira wale kuti abwere pafupi na iye, adawauza kuti, “Munthu an'funa kunditewera, abzilambe iye yekha, ndipo anyamule mtanda wace acinditewera.
Thangwe an'funa kupulumusa moyo wace, an'dzautaya, tsono wakutaya moyo wace thangwe ra Ine na Mafala Yabwino, an'dzaupulumusa.
Kodi ndiko kuti munthu ana phindu lanyi acikhala na bzentse bza pantsi pano, iye acitaya moyo wace?
Munthu kuti alombole moyo wace angapereke ciyani?
Nakuti aliwetse wa m'badwe wadzigololo na kuphonya uno, an'cita manyazi na Ine ndipombo na mafala yangu pamaso pa wanthu, napombo ine Mwana-wa-Munthu nin'dzacita naye manyazi pomwe nin'dzabwera pabodzi na anjo zakucena, na mbiri ya Baba wangu.”
Adawauza pomwe kuti, “N'cadidi ndiri kulewa kuti alipo winango pompano omwe an'dzafa lini akanati kuwona kufika kwa Umambo bwa Mulungu na mphambvu.”
Zatapita ntsiku zitanthatu, Jezu adatenga Pedru, Tiyagu na Juwau, acikwira nawo kuphiri litali kwa okha. Ndipo adasandusidwa Jezu pamaso pawo.
Bzakubvala bzace bzidasanduka bzicena, bziciyetima kuti mbe, kuposa momwe wakufula ali-yentse pa dziko angadacenesera.
Nthawe imweyo wakupfundzira wale adawona Eliya na Mozeji, alikuceza na Jezu.
Pedru adauza Jezu kuti, “Misiri, n'bzabwino kuti ife tikhale pano. Timange bzikumbi bzitatu, cibodzi canu, cinango ca Mozeji, na cinango ca Eliya.”
Akhalewa tenepo thangwe iye akhadziwa lini cakulewa sabwa iwo adabva mantha kwene-kwene.
Ndipo padafika mtambo uciwampsinkha. Mumtambomo mudabveka fala kuti:“Uyu ndiye Mwana wangu omwe nimbafuna, mum'bvere.”
Mwa cisututu, wakupfundzira wale pomwe adanyang'ana-nyang'ana, alibe kuwona wina, adandowona Jezu yekha.
Pomwe wakhabuluka m'phiri, Jezu adawaletsa kuti aleke kuwuza winango bzomwe adawona, mpaka Mwana-wa-Munthu amuke kwa wakufa.
Iwo adakoya cintsintsi cire, acimbabvudzana okha-okha kuti:“Kumuka kwa wakufa ndiko kulewa tani?”
Ndipo adambvundza aciti: “Kodi thangwe ranyi amisiri wa Mtemo ambalewa kuti Eliya an'dzakhala wakutoma kubwera?”
Jezu adatawira kuti: “N'cadidi, Eliya an'dzayamba kubwera kuti adzakondze bzentse. Tsono, thangwe ranyi bzakunemba bzimbalewa kuti Mwana-wa-Munthu an'dzaboneresedwa kwene-kwene na kunyozewa?
Tsono Ine ndiri kukuwuzani kuti Eliya adafika kale, ndipo wanthu winango adacita bzentse bzomwe iwo akhafuna ninga momwe Bzakunemba bzidalewera cipande ca iye.”
Pomwe iwo adabwerera kwa wakupfundzira winango wale, adawona mthithi ukulu wa wanthu ukhadawazungulira ndipo Amisiri wa Mtemo akhatsutsana na wakupfundzira wale.
Pomwe wanthu wentsenewo adawona Jezu, adadabwa kwene-kwene, ndipo adam'thamangira kukam'musa.
Iye adawabvundza kuti: “Nandi muli kutsutsana ciani?”
Ndipo m'bodzi wa wanthuwo adatawira kuti: “M'pfundzisi, ndakubwereserani mwana wangu wacimuna thangwe adaphatidwa na mzimu wakuipa wakumutazisa kulewa-lewa.
Ndipo ukandom'phata, umbam'gwesa pantsi, aciyamba kucoka phobvu kumulomo, acimbakukuta mano, mpaka thupi gwa kuuma. Ndipo ndidakumbira wakupfundzira wanu kuti aucose, tsono adatazira.”
Pamwepo Jezu adawatawira kuti, “Hu! Wanthu wakusaya cikhulupiriro! Nin'dzakhala namwe mpaka lini? Ndin'dzapirira namwe mpaka lini? ndibweresereni.”
wadabwera naye. Pakuwona Jezu, mzimu wakuipa udayamba kusukusa mulumbwana ule mwa mphambvu, mpaka iye pantsi khu, nkhumbabvumbvulika, acicoka phobvu kumulomo.
Jezu adabvundza baba wace kuti:“Bzimwebzi bzidamuyamba lini?” Baba wace adati:“Bzidamuyamba ali mwana.
Mzimu umweyu umbakhala ucimbamugwesa kawiri-kawiri. Umbam'gwesa pamoto pinango mmadzi kufuna kumupha. Penu Imwe mungakwanisa, tibvereni ntsisi, tithandizeni.”
Jezu adati:“Uli kuti mungakwanise, bzinthu bzentse n'bzakukwanisika kuna omwe ana cikhulupiriro.”
Pamwepo baba wa mwana adakuwa [acidandaula] aciti, “Ndiri kukhulupirira. Ndithandizeni kusaya cikhulupiriro kwangu.”
Pomwe Jezu adawona kuti wanthu ali kuwanda pambutoyo, adawutsimula mwa ukali mzimu wakuipayo, adati:“Iwe mzimu wakutazisa kulewa-lewa na kubva, ndiri kukuuza kuti ucoke mwa mwanayu, ndipo leka kudzapita pomwe mwa iye.”
Mzimu ule udakuwa ucim'sukusa mwa mphambvu, ucicoka. Mwana ule adakhala ninga wafa, mpaka azinji akhambati, “Wafa.”
Ndipo Jezu adam'phata boko acimuimisa, iye adaima.
Pomwe Jezu adakapita mnyumba, wakupfundzira wace adamubvundza pambali, kuti, “Ife tidatazira tani kuucosa mzimu ule?”
Jezu adatawira kuti, “Mzimu wa mtundu umweyu ungacoke lini pakusaya kucita mpembo [na kubzimana kudya].”
Jezu na wakupfundzira wace adacoka kumbuto ire ndipo adapita na kuGalileya. Iye akhafuna lini kuti wanthu adziwe komwe akhali,
thangwe akhapfundzisa wakupfundzira wace, acimbawati:“Mwana-wa-Munthu an'dzaperekedwa kwa wanthu, ndipo an'dzamupha. Tsono angamupha, Iye an'dzamuka pomwe zingadzapita ntsiku zitatu.”
Tsono iwo alibe kubvesesa bzomwe iye akhalewa, ndipo akhagopa kumubvundza.
Ndipo wadafika kuKafernau. Pomwe iye akhali mnyumba, adawabvundza kuti: “Kodi panjira pale mukhambatsutsana ciani?”
Wakupfundzira wale adakhala cete, thangwe bzomwe wakhatsutsana bzikhali bzakuti mkulu mbani pakati pawo.
Jezu adakhala pantsi, acicemera wakupfundzira khumi na awiri wale, aciwauza kuti:“Penu winango an'funa kukhala wakutoma, an'dzakhala wakumalizira, ndipo wakudzatumikira wentse.”
Pamwepo adatenga mwana m'bodzi, acimukhazika pakati pawo acikumbatira, adawauza kuti,
“Ali-yentse an'tambira mwana ninga uyu thangwe ra Ine, ali kutambira Ine, Ndipo wakutambira Ine, ali kutambira ine na omwe adandituma.”
Juwau adawuza Jezu kuti:“Mpfundzisi, ife tidawona munthu winango acimbacosa mizimu yakuipa pakulewa dzina lanu, ndipo tidamuletsa, thangwe ambafamba lini na ife.”
Tsono Jezu adati:“Lekani kumuletsa, thangwe palibe omwe angacite bzidabwiso mudzina langu patsogolo pace acindinyoza.
Sabwa wakusaya kutsutsana nafe, umweyo ngwakuphatana nafe.
Na tenepo ule omwe an'kupasani mkombo wa madzi mudzina langu, thangwe ra kuti ndimwe wa kwa Krixtu, cadidi ndiri kulewa kuti umweyo cipo angadzasaye kutambira mabaibai.”
“ Penu wina angaphonyese m'bodzi wa ang'onowa wakukhulupirira ine, umweyo bzikhali bwino kuti amangiriridwe cimwala ca nyampheyo mkhosi acikam'thusa panyandza.
Penu boko lako liri kukuphonyesa, ligwate. N'bzabwino kuti ukapite kumoyo wakusaya kumala uli wakugwatika boko, kuposa kuti ukapite una manja yentse mawiri kumoto wakusaya kumala.”
[“Kumweko kuna nkhonye zakuluma zimbafa lini, ndipo moto wacembo umbathima lini.”]
“Penu mwendo wako uli kukuphonyesa, ugwate. N'bzabwino kuti ukapite kumoyo wakusaya kumala uli wakugwatika mwendo, kuposa kuti ukathusidwe kumoto wakusaya kumala una miyendo yentse miwiri.”
[“Kumweko kuna nkhonye zakuluma zimbafa lini, ndipo moto wacembo umbathima lini.”]
“Penu diso lako liri kukuphonyesa, licose. n'bzabwino kuti ukapite muUmambo bwa Mulungu uli na diso libodzi lokha, kuposa kuti akakuthuse kumoto wakusaya kumala una maso yentse mawiri.
Kumweko kuna nkhonye zakuluma zimbafa lini, moto wacembo umbathima lini.
“Thangwe m'bodzi na m'bodzi an'dzalungidwa na moto.
Munyu ngwabwino, tsono ungaterepo wamala goso, umbadzakhala pomwe munyu? Moyo wanu ukhale na munyu, ndipo mukhale na mtendere imwe na andzanu.”
Ndipo Jesu adanyamuka pambuto ire, adayenda kumbali ya kuJudeya, kumbali ya ng'ambo ya mkulo wa Jordani. Ndipo wanthu azinji adadzagumana pomwe na iye. Mwa cizerewezi cace, akhawapfunzisa pomwe.
Ndipo adafika mafaliseu anango, adamubvundza kuti, “Nandi bzakubvumizidwa kuti munthu alambe m'kazi wace?” Akhadam'bvundza tenepo kuti amunyanganire thangwe.
Jezu adawatawira aciti: “Ciani comwe Mozeji adakulamulirani?”
Iwo adati:“Mozeji adabvumiza kuti munthu anembere m'kazi wace tsamba lakulambana patsogolo pace amucose.”
Jezu adati: “Mozeji adakunemberani mtemo umweyo thangwe ra kuuma mitima kwanu.
Koma, pa ciyambi pa bzentse Mulungu, adalenga wanthu, mamuna na m'kazi.
Thangwe race mwamuna an'dzasiya baba na mai, acikaphatana na m'kazi wace,
ndipo awiriwa akhala thupi libodzi. Na tenepo ndiwo lini pomwe awiri, akhala thupi libodzi.
Na tenepo bzomwe Mulungu waphataniza, munthu aleke kubzilekanisa.”
Pomwe adapita mnyumba, wakupfundzira adamubvundza Jezu bza nkhani imweire.
Iye adatawira kuti: “Omwe an'lamba m'kazi wace acikalowola munango, ali kucita upombo kuna mkazi wace.
Bzibodzi-bodzimbo m'kazi angalamba mwamuna wace, acikalowodwa na munango, na iyembo ali kucita upombo.”
Wanthu winango akhambabwera na wana kwa Jezu kuti awakhuye. Tsono wakupfundzira wace akhambawatsimula mwa ukali.
Jezu pomwe adawona bzimwebzire, adakalipa aciwauza kuti, “Alekeni wanawa abwere kwa Ine. Lekani kuwaletsa thangwe Umambo bwa Mulungu n'bwa wale wakulingana na iwowa.
Cadidi ndiri kulewa kuti omwe an'bvuma lini Umambo bwa Mulungu ninga mwana, umweyo an'dzabupita lini.”
Na tenepo adayamba kuwakumbatira wana wale, aciwasandzika boko na kuwadalisa.
Pomwe Jezu akhaguduka, munthu wina adam'thamangira, acimgodama kutsogolo kwace, acimubvundza kuti:“Mpfundzisi wabwino, kodi ningacite tani kuti ndidzatambire moyo wakusaya kumala?”
Jezu adamutawira kuti: “Uli kundicemereranyi wabwino? Wabwino ni m'bodzi yekha, Mulungu basi.
Mitemo umbaidziwa:‘Leka kupha, leka kucita upombo, leka kuba, leka kucita umboni bwakunama, leka kunamiza andzako, lemekeza baba wako na mai wako.’”
Munthu ule adati: “Mpfundzisi, bzentsenebzi nimbabziteweza kuyambira ndiri mwana.”
Jezu adamunyang'ana, na lufoi acimuwuza kuti:“Uli kusaya cinthu cibodzi: ndoko, ukagulise cuma centse. Kobiri zentse ukapase wanthu wakusauka, ndipo un'dzatambira cuma kudzulu. Patsogolo pace ubwere, udzanditewere.”
Pakubva bzimwebzi, nkhope yace idadodoma, ndipo adacoka na kuneseka mumtima thangwe akhali munthu wa nthaka izinji.
Jezu adanyang'ana mbali mwace, aciuza wakupfundzira wace kuti:“N'bzakunesa tani wacuma kukapita muUmambo bwa Mulungu!”
Wakupfundzira wadadabwa na mafalayo. Tsono Jezu adabwerezera, aciti:“Wana wangu, n'bzakunesa tani kukapita muUmambo bwa Mulungu!
N'bzakupusa kuti ngamira ipite pamubo wa ntsingano kuposa kuti munthu wakudala akapite muUmambo bwa Mulungu.”
Pamwepo wakupfundzira adadabwa kwene-kwene acibvundzana kuti:“Kodi angapulumuke mbani?”
Jezu adawanyang'ana aciti:“Kwa wanthu n'bzin'kwanisika lini, tsono kwa Mulungu ntenepo lini, Kwa Mulungu bzentse n'bzakukwanisika.”
Pamwepo Pedru adayamba kuuza iye, kuti:“Onani, ife tidasiya bzinthu bzentse kuti tikutewereni.”
Jezu adatawira:“Cadidi ndiri kukuuzani imwe, kuti omwe an'siya nyumba, abale, mpfumakazi, mai, baba, wana ayai minda thangwe ra Ine, ndipombo thangwe ra Mafala Yabwino,
umweyo pantsi pano an'dzatambira bzentse bzakuwanda kwene-kwene kusiyana na kale: nyumba, abale, mpfumakazi, mai, wana, minda, ndipombo matsautso. Ndipo kutsogolo an'dzatambira moyo wakusaya kumala.
Pamwepo azinji omwe ali wakuyamba an'dzakhala wakumalizira, wakumalizira an'dzakhala wakuyamba.”
Wakhali pa ulendo bwa kuJerusalemu, Jezu akhali patsogolo, wakupfundzira wace akhadabwa. Napombo wanthu omwe akhatewera akhana mantha. Ndipo adawacemera pomwe wakupfundzira khumi na awiriwo pambali, aciwafokotozera bzomwe bzin'dzamucitikira.
Adati:“Tiri paulendo wa kuJerusalemu. Kumweko Mwana-wa-Munthu ali kukaperekedwa kwa akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe na apfundzisi wa mtemo. Iwo an'kamutonga na kupasa nyathwa kuti aphedwe. Ndipo an'kamupereka kwa wanthu wakunja.
Iwo an'kamusinjirira, acikamupsipira mata, acimuchanga ndipo acimupha. Zingadzapita ntsiku zitatu, Iye an'dzamuka.”
Tiyagu na Juwau, wana wa Zebedeu, adafendera kwa iye aciti:“Mpfundsisi, comwe tinikukumbirani, muticitire.”
Jezu adabvundza kuti: “Mun'funa kuti ndikucitireni ciyani?”
Iwo adati:“Tin'funa kuti pomwe mun'dzakhala mumbiri yanu, mudzatiikhe m'bodzi kuboko lanu ladidi, wina lamadzere.”
Tsono Jezu adati: “Mun'dziwa lini bzomwe muli kukumbira. Kodi imwe mungakwanise kumwera mkombo omwe ine nin'dzamwera? Ndipo imwe mungadzabatizidwe ninga momwe ine nin'dzabatizidwa?”
Iwo adatawira kuti: “Inde, tin'dzakwanisa.” Pamwepo Jezu adati:“Cadidi, mkombo omwe Ine nin'dzamwera, imwe mun'dzaumwerambo, ndipo mun'dzabatizidwa ninga ine.
Tsono Ine ni utongi lini bwangu kuikha munthu kuboko ladidi ayai lamadzere. Mulungu ndiye adakondza mbutozo an'dzapasa ali-yentse omwe iye an'funa.”
Pomwe anango wale khumi adabva bzimwebzi, adakalipira Tiyagu na Juwau.
Ndipo Jezu adawacemera kuti abwere pafupi na iye, adati: “Mun'dziwa kuti atongi wa madziko ambayakunda. Akulu-akulu wawombo ambawonesa mphambvu zawo kwa wanthu wawo.
Tsono pakati pa imwe bzileke kukhala tenepo. Omwe an'funa kukhala mkulu, atumikire andzace.
Ndipo omwe an'funa kukhala wakuyamba, akhale kapolo wa wentse.
Thangwe Mwana-wa-Munthu: alibe kubwera kuti adzatumikiridwe tsono kuti Iye adzatumikire wanthu na kupereka moyo wace kuti alombole azinji.”
Ndipo atafika mumzinda wa Jeriko. Pomwe akhacoka mumzinda ule na wakupfundzira wace, pabodzi na mthithi wa wanthu, adagumana zimola m'bodzi wakukumbira-kumbira akhadakhala mphepete mwa njira. Munthuyo dzina lace akhacemeredwa Batolomeu, mwana wa Timeu.
Pomwe iye adabva kuti ni Jezu wa kuNazalee, adakuwa aciti:“Jezu, Mwana wa David, ndibvereni ntsisi!”
Wanthu azinji akhamutsimula mwa ukali kuti anyamale. Tsono iye adapitiriza kukuwa aciti:“ Mwana wa David, ndibverenimbo ntsisi!”
Jezu adaima, aciwauza kuti:“Mucemereni.” Iwo adamucemera acimuuza kuti: “Limba mtima, lamuka, ali kukucemera.”
Pamwepo iye adathusa kapote wace adamuka, acimoga, aciyenda kuna Jezu.
Jezu adamubvundza kuti: “Un'funa kuti ndikucitire ciyani?” Zimola ule adatawira kuti, “Mpfundzisi, nin'funa kuwona.”
Jezu adamuwuza kuti: “Ndoko, cikhulupiriro cako cakulimbisa.” Nthawe ibodzi-bodziyo adayamba kuwona, ndipo adatewera Jezu panjira.
Pomwe Jezu na wakupfundzira wace akhafendera kuJerusalemu, pafupi na mizinda ya Betefaje na Betaniya ya pafupi na phiri la oliveira, Iye adatuma wakupfundzira wace awiri,
aciti: “Ndokoni m'mui omwe uli kutsogolo kwanu. Mungandopita, mukagumana kabulu kadamangiridwa, komwe kakanati kupakiridwa na munthu ali yentse. Mukakatsudzule mucibwera nako.
Penu Wina an'kubvundzani kuti:‘Thangwe ranyi muli kucita bzimwebzi?’ Tawirani kuti: ‘Mbuya an'kafuna, ndipo patsogolo pace an'dzakabwezera pomwe kuno.’”
Panthawe yomweyo wakupfundzira wale adayenda, acikawona kabulu kadamangirira pafupi na msuwo, kunja mphephete mwa njira, ndipo adakatsudzula.
Anango omwe akhali pamwepo adawabvundza kuti: “Thangwe ranyi muli kutsudzula kabuluka?”
Iwo adawatawira ninga momwe Jezu adawauza. Ndipo adawaleka acitenga.
Wadakatenga kabulu, acibwera nako kuna Jezu ndipo wadatandika bzakubvala bzawo pamsana pakene, ndipo Jezu adapakira.
Wanthu azinji akhambatandika bzakubvala bzawo munjira, anango akhambatandika mithawi ya miti yomwe akhambatcola mminda.
Wanthu omwe akhali patsogolo, na omwe akhali mmbuyo, adakuwa kuti: “‘Ozana!’ Simbani omwe ali kubwera mudzina la Mbuya.
Simbani Umambo bwa baba wathu David, bomwe buli kubwera mudzina la mbuya. Ozana kwa Mulungu wakudzulu!”
Ndipo Jezu adapita muJerusalemu, acikapita muNyumba ya Mulungu. Pakuti yakhali kale maulo, adanyang'ana-nyang'ana bzentse ndipo adacoka aciyenda kuBetaniya pabodzi na wakupfundzira wace khumi na awiri.
Mangwana yace, pomwe iwo akhacoka kuBetaniya, Jezu adabva njala.
Ndipo na patali adawona mkuyu ukhana masamba. Adayenda pafupi kuti pinango angawone nkhuyu. Ndipo adafika, alibe kuwona nkhuyu, adandokawona masamba yokha. Nakuti ikhali lini nyengo ya nkhuyu.
Pamwepo adawuza mutiyo kuti:“Muti iwe, kuyambira lero, cipo winango ali-yentse an'dzadya lini bzisapo bzako.” Ndipo wakupfundzira wace adabva bzimwebzo.
Iwo atafika kuJerusalemu, Jezu adapita muNyumba ya Mulungu, aciyamba kuthotha omwe akhacita malonda mmwemo. Adagwesa meza zakusinthira kobiri na mipando ya wanthu wakugulisa nkhangaiwa.
Akhabvumiza lini ali-yentse agwate na pacinthalo ca Nyumba ya Mulungu adanyamula cinthu.
Ndipo akhawapfundzisa aciti:“Bzidanembedwa kuti: ‘Nyumba yangu in'dzacemeredwa Nyumba ya mapembero kwa madziko yentse.’ Tsono imwe mwaisandusa nkhunde ya mbabva.”
Pakubva bzimwebzi akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe na apfundzisi wa Mtemo akhanyang'ana njira yakuti amuphe. Tsono akhabva naye mantha thangwe wanthu wentse akhadabwa nabzo bzomwe Iye akhapfundzisa.
Kudayamba kudoka, Jezu na wakupfundzira wace adacoka mumzinda mule.
Macibese, pakuyenda munjira, adawona mkuyu ule wauma na mizi kubodzi.
Pamwepo Pedru pakumbuka bzire, adamuuza kuti:“Mpfundzisi, onani, mkuyu omwe mudatemberera wauma.”
Jezu adawatawira, “Khulupirirani Mulungu.
Cadidi ndiri kukuwuzani kuti penu wina aniuza phiri iri kuti: ‘Coka apa, ukabzithuse kunyandza,’ angalewa na mtima wakusaya kukayika, mucikhulupirira cadidi kuti bzomwe ali kulewabzo bzin'citika, na tenepo bzin'dzacitika ninga bzomwe walewa.
Na tenepo ndiri kukuwuzani kuti ciri centse comwe mungakumbire mwa kupemba, khulupirirani kuti mwatambira ndpo na tenepo mun'dzatambira.
Ndipo mungafuna kupemba, cakutoma mulekerere mwandzanu penu munaye cinthu. Mungaterepo, Baba wanu omwe ali Kudzulu an'dzakulekelerani bzakuipa bzanu.”
“Tsono penu imwe munilekerera lini andzanu, Baba wanu omwe ali Kudzulu an'dzakulekereranimbo lini bzakuipa bzanu.”
Adabwerera pomwe kuJerusalemu. Ndipo pomwe Iye akhandobzifambira mNyumba ya Mulungu, akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe, na apfundzisi wa mtemo, pabodzi na akulu wa maAjuda adabwera kuna iye acimubvundza kuti:
“Kodi utongi wakuti mumbacite bzimwebzi mudautenga kuponi? Mbani adakupasani utongi umweyu?”
Jezu adawatawira, “Na inembo ndicikupasani mbvundzo ubodzi. Munganditawira, ndipo nin'kuwuzani komwe ndidatenga utongi wakuti nimbacite bzimwebzi.
Kodi ubatizi bwa Juwau bukhali bwa kudzaulu ayai bwa wanthu? Nditawireni.”
Ndipo iwo adabvundzana acimbati, “Tingalewa adazitenga kwa Mulungu, umweyu anilewa kuti:‘Kodi thangwe ranyi tsono mulibe kum'khulupirira?’
Tsono tingalewa kuti adazitenga kwa wanthu...” Iwo akhagopa wanthu, pakuti wanthu wentse wakhatawirira kuti Juwau akhali mpolofita.
Na tenepo adamutawira Jezu kuti:“Tin'dziwa lini.” Iye adawatawira kuti:“Na inembo nin'kuwuzani lini komwe ndidautenga utongi wakuti nimbacite bzimwebzi.”
Patsogolo pace Jezu adawatsikira mathere. Adati, “Mwamuna m'bodzi adalima dimba la uva acimanga litsito kuzungulira dimbalo. Adacera dindi lakupsinyira uva, acimanga gota lakukhalilira dimbalo. Patsogolo pace adapasa alimi anango acipangana nawo kuti akabvuna ambam'pase bzisapo bzace. Ndipo iye adacoka mudzikomo.
Nthawe yakubvuna yatakwana, mwenekaciro adatuma wabasa wace kwa alimi wale kuti akatambire bzisapo bzace.
Tsono iwo adaphata wabasa ule acim'menya ndipo acimubweza alibe cinthu.
Mwenekaciro ule adatuma wabasa winango tsono alimi wale adam'tema mmsolo acimunyazisa.
Ndipo mwenekaciro ule adatuma wabasa winango iwo adamupha. Adacita bzibodzi-bodzi na wabasa azinji, winango adawamenya aciwapweteka, wina adawapha.
“Mwenekaciro ule adasala na mwana wace m'bodzi wapamtima. Ndipo patsogolo pace adadzam'tuma kuna iwo. Adakumbuka kuti, ‘Mwana wangu, an'kamulemekeza.’
Ndipo alimi wale adayamba kuwuzana kuti, ‘Omweyu ndiye nyanthaka wace. Mbatimuphe kuti idzakhale yathu.’
Cadidi adamuphata, acimupha acimuthusa kunja kwa dimbalo.
“Kodi mwenekaciro wa dimba an'dzacita ciyani? An'dzabwera aciwapha alimiwo, dimba lire acipasa anango.
Kodi mulibe kulewenga bzomwe bzakunemba bzimbalewa? Bzimbati, ‘Mwala omwe amisiri wakumanga nyumba adaulamba, ndiwo wadzakhala mwala wakufunika.
Mbuya Mulungu ndiye adacita, ndipo n'cidabwiso kwa ife.’”
Ndipo akulu wa Mayuda adadziwa kuti mathereyo akhayezerera iwo. Ndipopo adafuna kum'manga Jezu, tsono akhagopa mthithi wa wanthu. Ndipo iwo adandocoka acimuleka.
Wanthu wa bungwe la Afaliseyu, na winango wa phati ra Herodi adatumidwa kuti akatape mkanwa Jezu.
Iwo adafika aciti, “Mpfundzisi, tin'dziwa kuti imwe ndimwe wakulungama, ndipo mulibe lubvera. Mumbanyang'ana lini kuti uyu mbani, ndipo mumbapfundzisa njira ya uMulungu cadidi. Kodi kumbvumizidwa kuti timbapime msonkho kwa mambo wa kuRoma, ayai ne?
Timbapimedi ayai tileke?” Tsono Jezu pakudziwa ndzeru zawo zaciphamaso, adati:“Thangwe ranyi mundiyeza utowa? Ndipaseni kobiri ibodzi kuti ndiione.”
Iwo adam'pasa kobiri ire. Ndipo iye adawabvundza kuti, “Kodi nkhopeyi njayani, ndipo dzinali ndayani?” Iwo adatawira,“ Nbza Seza.’
Pamwepo Jezu adawauza kuti, “Ehedi! Perekani bza Seza kwa Seza, bza Mulungu kwa Mulungu.” Pakubva bzimwebzi adadabwa naye.
Pamwepo maSaduseu anango omwe ambati palibe an'dzamuka kwa wakufa, adafendera kwa Jezu. acimbvundza kuti:
“Mpfundzisi, Mozeji adatinembera kuti, ‘Penu munthu akafa, acisiya m'kazi, alibe naye mwana, m'bale wa wakufayo apite nthaka kuti abalire m'bale wace ule omwe adafa.’
Akhalipo wanthu anomwe paubale bwawo. Wakuyamba adalowola, adafa alibe kusiya mwana.
Waciwiri adapita nthaka, na iyembo adafa ne kusiya mwana. Bzibodzi-bodzi, bzidacitika kuna wacitatu.
Mpaka anomwe wentse adafa alibe kusiya wana. Pakumalizira mkaziyo adadzafambo.
Kodi pantsiku yakudzamuka kwa wakufa, mwenekaciro mkaziyo an'dzakhala uponi? Thangwe la kuti abale anomwe wale wentse akhadamulowola.”
Jezu adawatawira kuti, “Ndipopa mumbaphonya thangwe ra kusaya kudziwa bzakunemba ndipo na mphambvu za Mulungu.
Na tenepo pakumuka kwa wakufa, palibe kulowolana. Wentse an'dzakhala ninga anjo za Kudzaulu.
Tsono bzakuti wanthu an'dzamuka kwa wakufa, kodi mulibe kulewenga mulivu la Mozeji, pomwe pali kulewa bza citsamba cakugaka? Mulungu adamuwuza Mozeji kuti, ‘Ine ndine Mulungu wa Abramu, Izaki, na Jakobi.’
Ibzi bziri kulatiza kuti Mulungu ni mulungu lini wa wakufa, ni mulungu wa wamoyo. Imwepo muli kuphonyeka.”
Mdziwi m'bodzi wa mtemo, adabva kutsutsana kwawo. Pomwe adawona kuti Jezu adawatawira bwino Asaduseyu wale, adafendera adabvundza aciti, “Kodi mwa mitemo yentse, ukulu ni uponi?”
Jezu adamutawira kuti, “Mtemo ukulu nguyu, ‘Bvani, Aizirayeri! Mbuya, Mulungu wathu, ndiye Mulungu m'bodzi yekha.
Funa Mbuya, Mulungu wako, na mtima wako wentse, na moyo wako wentse, na ndzeru zako zentse, na mphambvu zako zentse.’
Mtemo waciwiri nguyu, ‘Funa andzako ninga momwe umbabzifunira iwe wekha.’ Palibe mtemo winango ukulu wakuposa mitemo imwei.”
Mdziwi ule wa mtemo* adati, “Mwatawira bwino, mpfundzisi. Ninga mwalewa, ncadidi kuti Mulungu ni m'bodzi yekha ndipo palibe winango.
Ndipombo umufune na mtima wentse, na ndzeru zentse, na mphambvu zentse, ndipombo funa mwandzako ninga umbabzifunira iwe wekha, bzimwebzi mpsabwino kuposa kupereka ntsembe zakutentha na ntsembe zinango zentse.”
Jezu adawona kuti munthuyo adatawira na udziwi. Ndipo adamuwuza kuti, “Iwe uli lini kutali na Umambo bwa Mulungu.” Kuyambira pamwepo pakhalibe winango wakulimba mtima kuti amubvundze.
Pomwe Jezu akhapfundzisa muNyumba ya Mulungu, adabvundza, “Kodi adziwi wa mtemo ambalewa kuti Krixtu ni mwana wa David?
Mwa mzimu wakucena David, adati: ‘Mbuya adawuza Mbuya wangu kuti ‘khala kuboko langu ladidi, mpaka ndiikhe awengi wako pansi pa minyendo yako.”
David caiye, ambacemera krixtu kuti, Mbuya. Angakhale tani mwana wace?” Wanthu azinji akhatetekera na kukomedwa kwene-kwene pakubva mafala yace.
Pomwe Jezu akhawapfundzisa, adati, “Cenjerani nawo adziwi wa mtemo. Ambafuna kuyenda adabvala bzakubvala bzitali nakuti alemekezedwe pamiseu.
Ambafuna mbuto yakutsogolo mnyumba zamapembero, ndipombo mbuto zakulemekezeka pauzokoto.
Ndipo ambawadyera nthaka za amansiwa, acimbacita mapembero matali-matali mwakunamiza. Wanthu omwewo andzapasidwa nyathwa ikulu.”
Ntsiku inango, Jezu akhadakhala pafupi na ntsengwa yakuikhira kobiri za ntsembe muNyumba ya Mulungu. Akhanyang'anisisa momwe wanthu akhaperekera kobiri zawo. Wanthu azinji wakudala akhathusa kobiri zizinji.
Tsono padafika mansiwa m'bodzi, adathusa tukobiri tuwiri twakukwanira quadrante .
Ndipo Jezu adacemera wakupfundzira wace aciwauza kuti, “Ncadidi ndiri kulewa kuti mansiwa wakusaukayu wathusa kuposa wanthu wentsewa omwe ali kuthusa kobiri muntsengwa.
Thangwe winangowa andothusa bzomwe atapa pa bzizinji anabzo. Tsono mkaziyu, mwa kusauka kwace, wathusa bzentse bzomwe akhali nabzo, napo bzomwe bzingadamuthandiza pamoyo wace.”
Pomwe Jezu akhacoka kuNyumba ya Mulungu, m'bodzi wa akupfundzira wace adamuwuza kuti, “Mpfundzisi, onani minyalayi na nyumbazi.”
Jezu adamuwuza kuti, “Kodi muli kuziwona nyumba zikulu-zikuluzi? Pan'dzasala lini mwala padzaulu pamwala undzace: yentse in'dzagumulidwa.”
Jezu adakhala pantsi paphiri la Olivera kutsogolo kwa Nyumba ya Mulungu. Ndipo Pedru, Tiyagu, Juwau na Andereya adamubvundza paokha kuti,
“Tiwuzeni bzimwebzi bzin'dzacitika lini? Tin'dzawona cizindikiro canyi kuti bziri pafupi kucitika?”
Pamwepo Jezu adawawuza kuti, “Cenjerani kuti wina ali-yentse aleke kukupumpsani.
Thangwe azinji an'dzabwera mudzina langu acimbadzalewa kuti, ‘Krixtu ndine.’ Ndipo wan'dzasoceresa wanthu azinji.
Mukadzabva nkhondo ayai ntabva-tabva wa nkhondo, lekani thupo. Bzimwebzi bzin'funika kuti bzidzacitike, tsono cimaliziro cikanati kufika.
Madzindza yakusiyana-siyana yan'dzasandukirana. Madziko yakusiyana-siyana yan'dzamenyana nkhondo. Mbuto zakusiyana-siyana zin'dzatekenyeka, ndipo kun'dzakhala njala. Tsono bzimwebzi bzidzakhala ninga kubvulumukidwa kwa mai wa pathupi.
“Cenjerani! Wanthu an'dzakuperekani kumbuto za kutongera mirandu, ndipo an'dzakuchangani mnyumba zamapemphero. Mun'dzawonekera kwa atongi na kwa azimambo thangwe ra Ine kuti mukandicitire umboni.
Ndipo bzakufunika kuti mafala yabwino ya yambe kulewedwa kwa wanthu wa madzindza yentse.
Ndipo angadzakuphatani acikuperekani pamphala, lekani kudzakhala na thupo kuti, ‘Kodi tikalewe ciyani?’ Mun'kalewa bzomwe Mulungu an'kakuwuzani panthawe yomweyo. Thangwe ndimwe lini mun'dzalewa-lewa. Mzimu Wakucena ndiwo un'dzalewa-lewa.
M'bale an'dzapereka m'bale wace kuti aphedwe. Baba, mwana wace. Wana an'dzasandukira azibaba wawo mpaka kuwaphesa.
Mun'dzawengedwa na wanthu wentse thangwe ra dzina langu. Ndipo omwe an'dzalimbika mpaka pakumalizira, ndiye an'dzapulumuka.”
“Mukawona cakudzonga cidaima pambuto yomwe cin'funika lini kuti cikhale. (Wakulewenga, abvesese!) Pamwepo omwe wali muYudeya adzathawire kumapiri.
Omwe ali pacigota, abuluke athawiretu. Aleke kupita mnyumba kuti akatenge cinthu.
Omwe ali kumunda, aleke kubwerera kunyumba kuti akatenge bzakubvala.
Tsoka kwa akazi omwe an'dzagumanizidwa ana pathupi na wakumamisa wana ntsiku zimwezo.
Mupembe kuti bzimwebzi dzileke kudzakuwonekerani pa nyengo ya mphepo
thangwe pantsiku zimwezo yan'dzawoneka mabvuto yomwe yakanati kuwoneka kucokera paciyambi ca dziko lapantsi mpaka lero, ndipo yan'dzawoneka lini pomwe.
Na tenepo Mbuya angadasaya kuzipunguza ntsikuzo, palibe omwe angadapulumuka. Tsono Mulungu adazipunguza thangwe ra wanthu omwe iye adasankhula.
“Na tenepo, winango angadzakuwuzani kuti, ‘Ali pano Krixtu,’ ayai ‘Uyo ali apo.’ Lekani kudzam'bvera
thangwe kun'dzawoneka wanthu wakunama an'dzalewa kuti, ‘Ndine Krixtu’ pinango kuti, ‘Ndine mpolofiti.’ Wanthuwo acimbadzacita mabasa yamphambvu ndipombo bzinthu bzakudabwisa kuti bzingadzakwanisika adzasocerese napo wakusankhulidwa na Mulungu.
Ndipo imwe khalani na tceru. Ine ndakuwuzani bzentsenebzi bzikhanati kuti bzicitike.”
“Ntsiku zimwezo, mabvutoyo yangadzamala, dzuwa lin'dzathima, mwezi un'dzaleka kugaka.
Nyenyezi zin'dzagwa kucokera kudzaulu, ndipo mphambvu za kudzaulu zin'dzatekenyeka.
Pamwepo an'dzawona Mwana-wa-Muntu ali kubwera mmitambo na mphambvu zikulu na mbiri.
Iye an'dzatuma anjo zace kuti akagumanize wakusankhulidwa wace kucokera kudziko lentse: kudzaulo, kunyantsi, kumabva dzuwa, na madokero”
“Pfundzirani kuna mkuyu. Mukawona kuti mithawi yace yayamba kuswipirira ndipo masamba yali kufundira, mumbadziwe kuti mayindza yafendera.
Na tenepo mungadzawona bziri kucitika, mudzadziwe kuti Mwana-wa-Munthu ali pafupi, ali pamsuwo caipo.
Cadidi ndiri kulewa kuti bzentsenebzi bzin'dzawoneka mbadwe uno ukanati kufa.
Kudzulu na dziko lapantsi bzin'dzamala, tsono mafala yangu yan'dzamala lini cipo.”
“Ndipo ntsiku na nthawe yace, palibe omwe aniidziwa. Anjo za kudzaulu zin'dziwambo lini. Napo Mwana an'dziwambo lini. Aniidziwa ni Baba ekha basi.
Cenjerani! Khalani wakupenya thangwe mun'dziwa lini nthawe in'dzakwana lini.
Bzin'dzakhala ninga mwenekaciro-nyumba omwe adacoka aciyenda ulendo. Ambasiya bzinthu mmanja mwa anyabasa wace, ali-yentse na basa lace, ndipo ambawuza mulindiri kuti akhale wakupenya.
Khalani wakupenya thangwe mun'dziwa lini nthawe yomwe mwenekaciro-nyumba an'dzabwera: penu ni maulo, penu ni pakati pausiku, penu ni congwe wakuyamba, ayai madandakweca.
Kuti angakwanise kudzabwera mwa cisututu, aleke kudzakugumanani mudagona.
Bzomwe ndiri kulewabzi, ndiri kuwuza mwentse ‘Khalani wakupenya.’”
Zikhadasala ntsiku ziwiri kuti ufike msinda wa Phasika na ntsiku yakudya mkate wakusaya cakutupisa. Akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe na apfundzisi wa Mtemo akhanyang'ana mpata wakuti amphate Jezu mwaciwembo, acimupha.
Tsono akhati:“Bzimwebzi tireke kubzicita panthawe ya cikondwereso kuti mbumba ileke kundzacita phokoso.”
Jezu akhali kuBetaniya akhadakhala paMeza, munyumba ya Sirimau nyamapere, adabwera mkazi mbondzi akhadanyamula ntsupa ya girazi, yamafuta yakununcira yakucokera ku muti wa narido*ya ntsengwa ikulu. Mkaziyo adaswa ntsupa ire, acitsanurira mumsolo mwa Jezu.
Ndipo wanthu winango adaipidwa nabzo waciuzana kuti, “Thangwe ranyi kuyadzonga tenepa mafuta yakununcira?
Angadayagulisa na ntsengwa yakupitirira kobiri zicena za nzayaya madzana matatu, acikapasa wakusauka” Na tenepo wanthuwo adamfufumira.
Tsono Jezu adati, “Mulekeni mkaziyu, muli kumuneseranyi? iye wandicitira basa labwino.
Thangwe wanthu wakusauka munawo nthawe zentse, pomwe mun'funa kuwacitira bza lufoi, mungakwanise kuwacitira. Tsono Ine mun'dzakhala lini nande nthawe zentse.
Omweyu wacita bzomwe angadakwanisa kucita. Wadzozerau thupi langu likanati kuikhidwa kuthenje.
Cadidi ndiri kukuuzani kuti kuli-kwentse padziko lapantsi komwe kungadzalalikidwe mafala Yabwino, bzidzafokotozedwambo bzomwe mkaziyu wacita kuti wanthu wamukumbukire.”
Judasi Iskaliote, m'bodzi wa wakupfundzira khumi na awiri wale, adayenda kwa akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe kuti akapereke Jezu kuna iwo.
Pomwe iwo adabva bzimwebzi adakomedwa ndipo wadapicira kuti an'dzamupasa kobiri. Pamwepo iye adayamba kunyang'ana mpata kuti apereke Jezu.
Pantsiku yakutoma ya msinda wa mikate yakusaya cakutupisa, ntsiku yomwe wanthu akhambapha mwana wa bira pakucita cikondwereso ca Phasika, wakupfundzira wa Jezu adamubvundza kuti, “Kodi tikakukondzereni kuponi mbuto yakudyera uzokoto wa Phasika?”
Jezu adatuma awiri mwa wakupfundzira wace, aciwauza kuti, “Ndokoni mumzindamu. Mun'gumana na mwamuna adanyamula mtsuko wa madzi. Mum'tewere.
Ndipo komwe an'kapita, mukauze mwenekaciro wa nyumba kuti, ‘Misiri ali kubvundza kuti, kodi n'ciponi cipinda cangu cakuti ndidzadyere uzokoto wa Phasika na wakupfundzira wangu?’
Iye an'kakuwonesani cipinda cikulu capadzaulu momwe akondza bzentse, mukatikondzere momwemo.”
Wakupfundzira wale adayenda acipita mumzinda mule. wadabziwona ninga momwe Jezu adawauzira ndipo wadakondza bza uzokoto bwa Phasika.
Kwatadoka, Jezu adabwera na wakupfundzira wace khumi na awiri wale.
Pomwe wakhadakhala pantsi acimbadya, Jezu adati, “Cadidi ndiri kulewa kuti mbodzi mwa imwe, omwe alikudya nande, an'dzandipereka kwa nyamadulanthaka wangu.”
Wakupfundzira wadabva wacidodoma. m'bodzi na m'bodzi adamubvundza kuti, “kodi ningakhale ine?”
Jezu adawatawira kuti, “Ni m'bodzi wa khumi na awirimwe omwe ali kuikha boko mundiro pabodzi nande.
Cadidi Mwana-wa-Munthu ali kukaphedwa ninga momwe bzidanembedwa. Tsono ana tsoka omwe an'kapereka Mwana-wa-Munthuyo. Bzikhali bwino kwa munthu umweyo angadasaya kubadwa.”
Ndipo pomwe iwo akhambadya, Jezu adatenga m'kate, aciudalisa, adagwata-gwata, acipasa wakupfundzira, ndipo adati, “Phatani, iri ni thupi langu.”
Patsogolo pace adatenga mkombo, acidalisa, adaupereka kwa wakupfundzira, wacimwa wentse.
Ndipo adawauza kuti, “Uyu ni mulopa wangu wa pangano la kulumbira. Mulopa omweyu ndin'dzawutaya thangwe la wanthu azinji.
Cadidi nin'kuuzani kuti, nin'dzamwa lini cakumwa ca muti wauvaci, mpaka ntsiku yomwe nin'dzamwa cipsa mu Umambo bwa Mulungu.”
Ndipo wadaimba nyimbo yakulemekeza Mulungu, adacoka waciyenda kuPhiri la Olivera.
Patsogolo pace Jezu adauza wakupfundzira wace kuti, “Mwentsenemwe usiku buno mun'disiya mucibwerera thangwe bzidanembedwa kuti, ‘Nin'dzapha makabusa ndipo mabira yan'dzabalalika.’
Tsono ndikadzamuka kwa akufa, nin'dzatsogola kuyenda kuGalileya.”
Ndipo Pedru adati, “Napo wentse wakusiyeni acibwerera, ine nibwerera lini cipo.”
Tsono Jezu adamuuza kuti, “Cadidi ndirikukuuza kuti lero usiku buno, congwe akanati kulira kawiri, un'dzandilamba katatu kuti un'ndidziwa lini.”
Pamwepo Pedru adagigimira kuti, “Napo bzicifunika kufa namwe pabodzi, cipo ningadzakulambeni kuti nin'kudziwani lini.” Anangowo wentse wadalewabo bzibodzi-bodzi.
Jezu adayenda na wakupfundzira wace kumbuto ibodzi, ikhacemerewa Gesemani*. Pomwe wadafika, Jezu adauza wakupfundzira wace kuti, “bakakhalani pano, Ine ndikapembe.”
Jezu adatenga Pedru, Tiyagu na Juwau. Iye adayamba kubva mantha makulu acidodoma.
Adawauza kuti, “mzimu wangu ngwakudodoma mpaka kufa. khalani mudapenya pano.”
Adayenda patsogolo pang'ono, adagodama pantsi, acipemba kuti penu n'bzakukwanisika nthawe yakugoswa ire imupitirire.
Adapemba kuti:“Aba, Baba, bzinthu bzentse bzingakwanisike kwa imwe. Mucose mkombo wa matsautsoyu kwa ine, tsono lekani kucita bzomwe ine ninfuna, citani cifuniro canu.”
Atabwerera kuna wakuphunzira wace adawagumana wadagona. Ndipo iye adabvundza Pedru kuti, “Sirimau, uli kugona kodi? Cadidi watazira kukhala udapenya panthawe ibodzi yokha?
Khalani mudapenya mucimbapemba, kuti muleke kuyezedwa na bzakuipa. Cadidi mzimu uli kufuna, tsono thupi lawofoka.”
Adayenda pomwe kapemba na mafala mabodzibodzi yale.
Pomwe adabwerera, adawagumana adagona, thangwe bzikhope bzawo bzikhadalemedwa na tulo. Na tenepo iwo adasaya cakumtawira.
Pomwe adabwerera kacitatu, adati, “Kodi muli kugona na kupuma? Bzakwana. Nthawe ire yakwana, Mwana-wa-Munthu ali kukaperekedwa kwa wanthu wakuipa.
Mukani, mbatiyende. Onani wa kundipereka kwa nyamadulanthaka ule, wafika.”
Jezu akanati kumaliza kulewa-lewa, nthawe yomweyo adafika Judasi, m'bodzi wa wakupfundzira khumi na awiri wale. Adabwera na mthithi wa wanthu akhadanyamula bzisenga na mabonga. Wanthuwo adatumidwa na akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe na apfundzisi wa Mtemo na akulu wa Ajuda.
Wakudzam'pereka ule akhadawauza cizindikiro ca kuti, “Omwe nin'kapsompsonayo, ngumweyo. Mun'kam'phate mun'ciyenda naye, lekani kamuleka.”
Pomwe Judasi adabwera, adandofika pana Jezu adati, “Misiri!” Ndipo adamumpsompsona.
Ndipo wanthu wale adam'phata Jezu wacimmanga.
Tsono mbodzi mwa wakupfundzira omwe akhali naye pamwepo, adasolola cisenga cace, adapweteka wabasa wa mkulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe, ndipo adam'gwata khutu.
Tsono Jezu adawabvundza wanthu wale kuti, “ mwandibwerera na bzisenga na mabonga kudzandimanga ninga ndine mbava?
Ntsiku zentse ndikhakhala namwe ndicimbapfundzisa muNyumba ya Mulungu, imwe nee kundiphata. Tsono bzimwebzi bzakukwanirisa bzomwe bzidanembedwa.”
Pamwepo wakupfundzira wace wentse wadamsiya wacibwerera.
Mulumbwana m'bodzi akhadafunika ciriya akhatewera Jezu. Wanthu wale akhafuna kuphata,
tsono iye adaikopola nguwo ire, acithawa ali pezi.
Ndipo iwo adatenga Jezu aciyenda naye kunyumba ya mkulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe. Kumweko kukhadagumana wentse akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe na akulu wa Ajuda, na apfundzisi wa Mtemo.
Pedru akhamutewera Jezu na patali, mpaka iye adakapitambo ku seri kwa nyumba ya mkulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe kule. Adakhala pantsi pabodzi na walindiri aciwotha moto.
Akulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe wale na wentse akulu wa mbuto ikulu ya Majuda akhanyang'ana umboni wakupasa mulandu Jezu kuti amuphe. Tsono alibe kuuwona.
Azinji akhambalewa bzakumnamizira. Tsono umboni bwawo bukhabverana lini.
Winango wadaima waciyamba kumbalewa bzakunama.
waciti, “Munthu uyu ife tidamubva acimbalewa kuti, ‘Ine nin'dzapfudza Nyumba ya Mulunguyi yakumangidwa na wanthu. Ndipo muntsiku zitatu nin'dzamanga inango yakusaya kumangidwa na wanthu.’”
Napo tenepoyo uboni bwawo bukhabverana lini.
Ndipo mkulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe adaima pamaso pawo, acibvundza Jezu kuti, “Kodi ulibe cakutawira? N'bziponi bzomwe wanthuwa wali kukunamizira?”
Jezu adanyamala. Alibe kudzatawira pomwe. Pamwepo mkulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe ule adabvundza pomwe kuti,“Kodi ndiwe Crixtu Mwana wa Mulungu wakusimbiwa?”
Jezu adatawira kuti, “Inde, ndine. Ndipo mun'dzawona Mwana-wa-Munthu adakhala kuboko ladidi la Mulungu wamphambvu zentse. Mun'dzamuwona ali kubwera mmitambo yakudzulu.”
Pamwepo mkulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe ule adang'amba bzakubvala bzace, acilewa, ‘tin'funiranyi pomwe mboni?
